Current Commentary

Thoughts on the Passing of Poincaré 16

— Heng

丨France's Future Diplomacy丨

Since this summer, there have not only been many events in European countries, but also the deaths of their political figures have been more frequent than usual. Among them, people such as Hindenburg died of old age, and Dollfuss, Alexander, and Barthou all died by assassination. The world has been shocked by the deaths of these people, fearing that the international situation may change dramatically as a result. Unexpectedly, a European telegram reported that the old French politician Poincaré had also passed away. How can the world not be filled with sorrow and feel that France, as the center of the European situation, has lost two major political figures in one week, making people lament endlessly.

Poincaré served as the President of France for seven years (1912-1920), but he was not as well-known to the world as when he was the Prime Minister, especially when he concurrently served as the Minister of Foreign Affairs. The President of France is a position of honor, and in reality, the political issues of great importance are handled by the Prime Minister. Therefore, once elected as President, their name often cannot be seen in the newspapers every day. As is the case with Doumergue today, he once served as President (1920-1927), but few know it. Now that he is the Prime Minister, more people know him. This is because one wields real power and the other holds a nominal position. However, the name of the Prime Minister is sometimes far less dazzling than that of the Foreign Minister. Because in this time of international turmoil, if its Foreign Minister has talent, he will undoubtedly be able to establish extraordinary achievements with superior skills. Internally, he receives praise from the people, and externally, he receives respect from other countries. The late Briand and the recent Barthou had both served as Prime Minister many times, but their fame in the world was during their time as Foreign Minister. The facts are obvious. Poincaré's fame also lies in his concurrent position as Prime Minister and Foreign Minister, not in his position as President of France.

Since the Great War, there have been three people in France whose diplomatic achievements shook the world: one is Poincaré, the second is Briand, and the third is Barthou. Poincaré's diplomacy was uncompromising towards Germany. The treaty must be fulfilled, and reparations must be paid. Although it was difficult to cope with the lack of cooperation from Britain at the time, he still did not hesitate to use force to pressure Germany and send troops to occupy the Ruhr. Other notable aspects of his policy towards Germany included the prolonged failure to withdraw troops from the Rhineland and the refusal to reduce the amount of reparations. Therefore, Poincaré's diplomacy is the most rigid type of French diplomacy. As for Briand's diplomacy, the world knows that it was diplomacy of cooperation and harmony. The conclusion of the Locarno Treaty, Germany's joining the League of Nations, the establishment of the Non-Aggression Pact, and the reduction of German reparations are all major diplomatic achievements. The most recent Barthou was a diplomatic master of both alliance and division. His purpose was to ally with many countries to isolate Germany. Examples include strengthening the alliance of the Little Entente, promoting the unity of the Balkans, creating a Franco-Russian alliance, eliminating Anglo-French suspicions, and dispelling Franco-Italian suspicions. These are all his great successes. This type of diplomacy can be called group diplomacy or alliance diplomacy. In short, although the diplomatic styles of these three people seem to be different, their main purpose is the same. Poincaré's intention was to prevent Germany from rising again to cause trouble for France. Briand's main purpose was to eliminate the hatred of the Germans and restore them to friendship in order to seek understanding between the two countries. Barthou's intention was to build more friendly nations to reduce German assistance. Therefore, in a word, the efforts of the three were all to seek security for France, but their methods were slightly different.

Now Barthou is gone, and his position as Foreign Minister has been succeeded by Laval. Poincaré is gone, and his person is only left in the imagination of French political history. Will France's diplomacy continue as before or will it open up a new path? This is a question that deserves attention. However, based on a general observation of French diplomacy over the past ten years, its fundamental point is always security, and its methods are no more than these three paths: rigidity, cooperation, and alliance. Moreover, the diplomatic policies of the various parties in France are largely the same, so the political tides in the past were all about internal affairs, and political tides rarely occurred due to diplomacy. And in times of national difficulty, the direction of diplomacy must be determined and unwavering. Therefore, changes in people will not have much impact. If there is any, it will only be in the difference in skills and not in other areas. This is what we can imagine and obtain.

Philippine Hurricane Blowing Northwest, Approaching Our South China Sea Area, Yangtze River Area Not to be Affected 17

Manila's Disaster Situation is Extremely Serious

Millions of Dollars in Material Losses

(Nanjing) According to information from the Central Meteorological Research Institute, the typhoon that occurred yesterday in the southwestern waters of the Philippines has now reached the western part of the island, approaching our South China Sea area. Its center is between 17 degrees north latitude and 118 degrees east longitude, and it is moving northwest. The Gulf of Guangzhou will be affected, and the Yangtze River basin will not be affected. (17th Central News Agency dispatch)

(Manila) This wind disaster is the worst in ten years, with 39 deaths, 40,000 homeless, 7,350 houses destroyed, and losses of US$1 million. Manila's commerce has returned to normal this morning. The floods that came with the hurricane yesterday have also receded today, but streetcars have not yet started running. The Manila Electric and Railway Company estimates that the company's losses are over 200,000 pesos. The victims this time, except for one unidentifiable American, are all Filipinos. Inland waterway transportation resumed this morning. (17th National Telegram)

Border Disputes Erupt Amidst Deteriorating Relations Between Hungary and Yugoslavia 18

Hungarian Man Shot Dead by Yugoslavian Border Guards, Public Outrage Ensues

France and Yugoslavia Share Hardships, Friendship Strengthens Over Time

Before the Remote Causes of the Marseille Incident Are Clarified

Yugoslavia Temporarily Refrains From Diplomatic Action

Budapest: Yesterday, a Hungarian man named Kolake was shot dead by Yugoslavian guards when crossing the Yugoslavian border. Upon hearing this news, public outrage has erupted. Earlier this year, Hungary and Yugoslavia had a dispute over border issues, which was brought before the League of Nations. There are concerns that a similar dispute will occur again. (Reuters, 17th)

Belgrade: Since the Marseille assassination, the government has not yet decided what diplomatic actions it will take regarding this case. This is the opinion of responsible figures in Yugoslavia. They believe that a decision can only be made after the investigation is clear and the remote and immediate causes of the assassination are understood. Therefore, as of now, no preparations have been made for any kind of negotiations, whether with Hungary or Geneva. (Havas, 16th)

Belgrade: A spokesman for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs declared to our reporter that France and Yugoslavia are allied countries, sharing hardships together, and their friendship grows stronger over time. Now that the French President has come to this country, the people of Yugoslavia will treat him as a close friend. "The friendship between France and Yugoslavia will never be broken. The arrival of the French head of state will only make the relations between the two countries even closer." The spokesman's statement can represent the unanimous opinion of all sectors of Yugoslavia, that is, both France and Yugoslavia have been harmed by the Marseille tragedy. The friendship between France and Yugoslavia has become stronger since the European War. During the Battle of Salonika, French and Yugoslav soldiers fought side by side, their blood staining the battlefield. (Note: During the European War, after Bulgaria joined the German-Austrian alliance, Serbia was attacked from both sides, and the Serbian army retreated into Albania. Later, British and French troops landed in Salonika, Greece, and the Serbian army joined them in combat.) The people of both countries will never forget this. Now, another tragedy has occurred, causing the leaders of both countries to suffer untimely deaths. The friendship between the two countries will become even closer as a result. (Havas, 16th)

Former King of Yugoslavia's Funeral Today: Political Enemies Abandon Old Grudges, National Feeling Runs High 19

French President and Romanian King Arrive in Capital to Pay Respects

Hitler Sends Goering to Attend the Funeral

Belgrade: Since Tuesday morning, countless people have been flocking to pay their respects to the late King Alexander. The place where the coffin rests is surrounded by white chrysanthemums, creating a somber atmosphere. The dim candlelight further enhances the sense of sorrow. Black tassels hang low around the coffin, behind which is a large white cross, below which is placed the crown, still shining brightly. Many of the mourners, both women and men, have been waiting for so long that they are unable to stand it any longer. Representatives of the German minority in the country have also presented four wreaths. The King's funeral is scheduled for tomorrow, with representatives from twenty-seven countries participating. (National Telegram, 17th)

Belgrade: Former Prime Minister of Yugoslavia and leader of the Croatian People's Party, Dr. Kraulischetz, who was the most vehement opponent of King Alexander, will also come here to attend the funeral. People in Yugoslavia are greatly moved by this. Dr. Kraulischetz also issued a declaration in Spalato last Sunday, renouncing his opposition policy forever, which shows that his words are sincere. The late King's other political enemies, Dr. Spaco and Dr. Krasnicai, will also come here, which is also seen as a sign of abandoning old grudges. It is noted that the two men are leaders of Yugoslav Muslims. (National Telegram, 17th)

Belgrade: French President Lebrun arrived here at 8:30 this morning. The Yugoslav Regent, members of the government, and personnel from the French embassy all went to the station to greet him. After reviewing the honor guard, the President went to the palace to meet with Romanian King Carol. The special train carrying French troops to Yugoslavia to attend the funeral of the late King arrived at 9:30 a.m. The Yugoslav officials and people welcomed them warmly. (Havas, 17th)

Belgrade: Nineteen French military aircraft participating in the funeral of King Alexander I of Yugoslavia, led by Lieutenant Colonel Kilian and Major Weisel, arrived in Yugoslavia today. The aircraft personally piloted by French Minister of Aviation Tran, as well as two other aircraft, will arrive tomorrow.

(Havas, 16th)

(Berlin): German leader Hitler, in his capacity as Supreme Commander of the Armed Forces, today appointed Prussian Prime Minister General Goering as the special envoy to attend the funeral of King Alexander I of Yugoslavia. Goering will fly to the capital of Yugoslavia tomorrow morning, accompanied by Lieutenant General Braschkowitz and Navy Captain Baron Holtzdorf. The government also issued a statement tonight regarding this matter, stating that the German leader wanted to show the German military's respect for the late King of Yugoslavia, and therefore sent his most trusted person as a special envoy. Goering will present a wreath at the tomb of the late King in the Yugoslav capital, with the inscription: "The German military respectfully offers this with deep sorrow at the tomb of a former valiant enemy." (National Telegram, 16th)

Origins of Marseille Assassination Suspects Ascertained 20

Kalman Is Actually Joseph's Alias

Committed the Crime After Being Granted Amnesty, Joined Terrorist Group

Sofia: The real name of Kalman, the assassin of the King of Yugoslavia, is Joseph, also known as Chernozemsky, nicknamed "Driver" Prahda. He is a well-known Macedonian terrorist, whose identity has been confirmed by the Yugoslav police. It has now been proven without a doubt that the fingerprints of Kalman sent by the French police have been compared with the fingerprints of Joseph and are indeed consistent. (Havas, 16th)

Belgrade: The Minister of the Interior has recently received a report proving the name and origin of the assassin of the late King Alexander. The tattoo on the left arm of the assassin Kalman, the scars on his abdomen, and the fingerprints left by the police in Sofia in 1931, all prove that the criminal Kalman is indeed Joseph, also known as Chernozemsky, a member of the Macedonian rights terrorist party. This person left the capital of Yugoslavia in 1932 and went to the capital of Hungary, where he stayed and served the party. (National Telegram, 17th)

(Paris): The National Investigation Team has recently obtained new information regarding the origins of the assassin Joseph, also known as Kalman. It has been learned that Joseph was born in 1897 in the Macedonian region belonging to Serbia. At the age of fourteen, he followed his mother to Bulgaria and worked as a car driver. He then changed his profession to transportation and joined the Bulgarian "Olymp" revolutionary organization. In 1924, he assassinated parliamentarians Demov and Domarewski. He was later arrested and sentenced to death. In 1932, he was granted amnesty and left Bulgaria to join the Yugoslav Croatian terrorist organization (organized by parliamentarian Pavletic). (Havas, 16th)

Captured Criminal Confesses Accomplices: Melun, France: The small police station in Melun, 28 miles southeast of Paris, was visited today by a Yugoslav police chief to examine Marni, (also known as Cherny), the suspect in the Marseille assassination who was arrested there yesterday. He confirmed that the man was his former driver. The criminal confessed that his real name was Kraguy, born in Yugoslavia in 1908. He was ordered to assassinate King Alexander of Yugoslavia. He was indeed next to Kalman on the day of the crime, but he did not participate because he was afraid. (Reuters, 16th)

Three of Seven Fugitives: Melun, France: After Marni was arrested, he was questioned by Simonovic, the head of the investigation team from the capital of Yugoslavia, from 6 p.m. until 1:30 a.m. Marni has confessed to participating in the conspiracy. His nickname among the party members is "Cherny," meaning "strongman." He was ordered to strike in Paris or Marseille when the opportunity arose. So far, there seem to be a total of seven accomplices to the assassin. In addition to the main assassin Joseph (also known as Kalman) who was killed on the spot, Novak (also known as Pospisil) and Penes (also known as Reichlick) have been imprisoned, and Marni has also been arrested. The remaining fugitives are the beautiful woman Utrov and two other men. It is estimated that the leader of the party is among the two men who have not yet been captured. (Havas, 16th)

Mysterious Woman Missing: Marseille: The police here recently conducted an inspection of the hotel in Aix where Marni and the beautiful woman Utrov were staying. As a result, two bombs and a pistol were found in Marni's room. These bombs were identical to those found on the main assassin Joseph (also known as Kalman), which shows that Marni's participation in the conspiracy is confirmed. As for the beautiful woman Utrov, her whereabouts are still unknown. (Havas, 16th)

US and Japanese Representatives Arrive in London, Naval Talks to Commence Soon, Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Expresses Stance 21

(London): Important talks will resume this week as preparation for convening the London Naval Conference next year. Representatives of various naval powers have now gathered here. US representative Davis, US Naval Tactics Director Standley, and Japanese representative Yamamoto all arrived in London last night. (Reuters, 17th)

(Tokyo): Representatives of various countries for disarmament have arrived in London, and the naval preparatory conference will open soon. The following statement was issued on the 16th, declaring Japan's beliefs: (1) Establishment of the right to national self-defense. Each country has the inherent right to maintain sufficient military strength to ensure its national defense. Japan has the inherent right to maintain sufficient military strength to ensure its national defense, and it is a necessary obligation to ensure peace in the Far East. (2) Achievement of substantial disarmament. Japan advocates for the reduction of armaments, not the expansion of armaments. In other words, based on the spirit of disarmament, we will do our best to reduce the armaments of various countries in order to reduce the burden on the people and promote friendly relations between countries. (3) Reduction of offensive weapons. Various countries should completely abolish offensive weapons in order to establish the principle of non-aggression. In accordance with the principle of strengthening defensive weapons, we will implement the reduction of armaments. (4) Abolition of the Washington Treaty and conclusion of a new treaty. Japan will abolish the Washington Treaty and hopes to conclude a fair and appropriate treaty to replace the old treaty. (5) Measures in case the treaty is not concluded. If an agreement cannot be reached, Japan will take measures to properly handle its national defense. However, Japan is determined to conduct negotiations in a peaceful manner from beginning to end, and strive to avoid the deterioration of international peace. (United Press, 17th)

(London): Japanese representative to the London Naval Preparatory Talks, Rear Admiral Yamamoto, arrived in Southampton at 4:30 p.m. today. British and Japanese officials welcomed him at the port. The British Minister of the Navy was represented by Admiral Jackson. After a short rest, Yamamoto boarded a train to London, arriving here at 7:40 p.m. Ambassador Matsudaira and personnel from the Japanese embassy, as well as leaders of the British government, greeted him at the station. Yamamoto told foreign reporters today that Japan will do its best to make the naval conference a success. (National Telegram, 16th)

(London): Regarding the naval conference preparatory talks, although the British side has announced that it plans to hold separate talks between the two countries, it is generally believed that it would be better for the representatives of the UK, US, and Japan to hold joint talks immediately. Those around US Chief Representative Davis do not conceal this view. However, in terms of due process, the US side believes that since the naval talks were initiated at the invitation of the UK, it is appropriate to follow the methods decided by the UK. (Havas, 17th)

(Moscow): Izvestia commented on the preliminary naval talks to be held in London, saying, "On the one hand, Japan has declared that it wants to abolish the Washington Treaty, and on the other hand, the United States has declared that it wants to maintain the Washington and London Agreements. These two demonstrative and conflicting declarations reaffirm the fact that the second preliminary naval talks, in terms of whether they can conclude any specific agreement, will open under extremely unfavorable conditions. Behind the issues of submarines and aircraft carriers lies a fundamental modern issue, namely the general relationship between the navies of Japan and the UK and the US. "The political significance of Japan's demands is to conclude a special treaty with the United States, creating a situation that forces the United States to give up its influence in Asian affairs. This has angered the United States, which is unwilling to abandon its plans to gain influence in China and other Asian countries. Therefore, it is also in a similar state of conflict. It is easy for us to see that whether the London talks have a chance of success is even more questionable." (TASS, 16th)

(London): A faction of the Conservative Party not only looks down on the initial naval talks, but also does not value the naval conference itself. These people fear that the British government may endanger national security by making concessions during the preliminary talks and the formal conference. Among them, the Morning Post stated that some cabinet members are deeply afraid that Prime Minister MacDonald is paying too much attention to the issue of rapprochement between Japan and the United States, and is willing to make concessions to the United States. It should be firmly stated that the British navy is inferior due to existing treaty relations, which Britain cannot tolerate for long. The Daily Mail, on the other hand, used sarcastic language, saying that the naval talks are precarious, and that what is currently being discussed are issues such as the limitation of total tonnage, the maximum tonnage of battleships, and the deployment of naval forces. It is hoped that the next war will make it clear to people that the ratio system, which experts pay so much attention to, is not reliable in modern warfare, because the power of submarines and aircraft can invalidate the ratio system. Experts do not seem to have seen the birth of submarines and aircraft. (Havas, 17th)

Struggle to Control Puppet State, Japanese Cabinet Decides to Maintain Original Plan, Military Rule Advocated Wins Again, Hishikari Uses Military Force to Suppress Kwantung Office 25

(Tokyo): The fate of the Japanese cabinet now hinges on the dispute over the Japanese administrative system in Manchuria. The cabinet is scheduled to hold a special meeting at 3:00 p.m. today to resolve this major dispute. It is widely believed that the cabinet will reaffirm its support for the reorganization plan in Manchuria, but it is impossible to fully satisfy the three opposing parties, as Minister of War Hayashi has refused to mediate, and the Kwantung Office and the Colonization Ministry have announced that they are determined to stick to their guns. This situation is unprecedented in Japanese history. (Reuters, 17th)

(Tokyo): The emergency cabinet meeting on the 17th opened at 3:00 p.m. After careful discussion on the issue of reforming the organization stationed in Manchuria, it was finally decided to forcibly order its implementation in accordance with the government's original plan. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 p.m. (United Press, 17th)

(Tokyo): On the 17th, at the cabinet meeting, regarding the issue of reforming the organization stationed in Manchuria, the government decided to clarify its attitude and issue a statement in the name of the Chief Cabinet Secretary. The statement reads as follows: In order to adjust the organizations related to Manchuria, a case was decided at the cabinet meeting on the 14th of this month, and preparations are being made to proceed in accordance with this resolution. In the 16th and 17th cabinet meetings, we considered how to handle the actual situation and other related matters. The government will handle the matter in accordance with the policy that has been decided, and will remain consistent and will not change. In the future, it will be necessary to promote the necessary laws and regulations in order to establish the adjustment of organizations related to Manchuria. Recently, it has been heard that there are concerns that this plan will turn the police into gendarmerie. It is not known that this method was originally intended to unify the command system, and it is by no means intended to turn the police into gendarmerie. Therefore, there should be no misunderstanding or anxiety about this point. We hope that all parties involved will thoroughly understand the fundamental purpose of this case, eliminate past misunderstandings, and enable the government to smoothly implement its policy towards Manchuria. (United Press, 17th)

(Tokyo): Based on the decision made at the cabinet meeting on the 17th, regarding the issue of concurrent appointments, the government respects the position of the Kwantung side and issued the following legalization policy: (1) The new organization's police department will have four sections: police affairs, security, higher education, and health. (2) Among them, the security department is directly related to military affairs because it maintains law and order and suppresses bandits. Therefore, a military officer should be appointed as the head of the section, and some soldiers should also be added to its staff. (3) Among the higher education staff, in order to maintain contact in terms of the nature of the affairs, a gendarmerie officer of the rank of lieutenant should also be added. (4) The person in charge of personnel administration for police officers is the police affairs section, and its section chief should be appointed by a civilian official with the rank of imperial appointment, placing him above the heads of the various sections. No soldiers may be added to the police affairs section or the health section. (United Press, 17th)

(Tokyo): Prime Minister Okada, based on the decision made at the cabinet meeting, is seeking ways to appease the Kwantung side, and the Colonization Ministry and the Army are separately issuing orders to the area, hoping that they will exercise self-control. (United Press, 17th)

(Changchun): Kwantung Army Commander Hishikari summoned the directors of the three bureaus, Hishita (Internal Affairs), Nakamura (Finance), and Ohba (Police Affairs), to Changchun, demanding that they pacify the Kwantung Office officials. If the three bureau directors do not comply, he will resolutely suppress them with military force. (Electric News, 17th)

Anci County Suffers Flood Damage Due to Autumn Rains 63

(Tianjin) In Anci County, southern Hebei, continuous autumn rains have caused the river waters in the county's second district, including Ge Yucheng, Han'erhe, Linjia Chang, and Majia Chang, and over ten villages to overflow their banks due to the rising water levels, inundating the wheat seedlings over an area of more than twenty li, turning them into a waterlogged area. Over ten thousand affected farmers in the villages have elected representatives such as Guo Hongnian and over ten others to come to Tianjin to petition the provincial government, pleading for prompt allocation of relief funds. (Seventeenth dispatch)

Number of Kailuan Tangshan Miners 64

(Tianjin) According to a survey by the Tangshan Public Security Bureau of Kailuan Tangshan miners, there are currently 5,750 people, 6,677 people in the Majiagou mine, 12,495 people in the Zhaogezhuang mine, 9,526 people in the Linxi mine, and 424 people in the Tangjiazhuang Third Mine. The five mines have a total of 38,672 workers. Qixin Cement Company has 3,221 workers, the magnetic factory has 655 workers, and the Beining Railway Factory has 3,824 workers. In addition, there are 2,054 workers in spinning mills and small factories, 2,639 iron machine workers, 130 leather workers, and 156 weaving and dyeing workers. The city has a total of 51,829 workers, accounting for 7/10 of the population. (Seventeenth dispatch)

Yellow River Conservancy Association to Hold General Assembly Today 65

(Tianjin) Li Yizhi, Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, has arrived in Tianjin. The General Assembly is scheduled to convene at 9:00 AM on the 18th in the Provincial Government Auditorium. Today, the General Affairs Office continued to receive proposals from the construction departments of various provinces, which have been included in the agenda. (Seventeenth dispatch)

(Tianjin) Li Yizhi, Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, stated that he went to Suiyuan, Gansu, Ningxia, and other places in mid-September to investigate and study water conservancy and navigation on the upper reaches of the Yellow River. Navigation has now been opened from Ningxia to Baotou, but the river surface varies in width, with some narrow sections only twenty or thirty meters wide and rapid currents, making dredging difficult. Shanxi province built small-wheeled boats with a draft of two feet to travel back and forth, which can only carry ordinary passengers and cargo to maintain transportation. The Yunting Canal in Ningxia province and the Minsheng Canal in Suiyuan province have greatly benefited agricultural water conservancy. This time, a fundamental plan for canal water conservancy is needed, so a meeting in Tianjin is necessary. (Seventeenth dispatch)

(Hankou) According to the evening news, Yu Xuezhong visited Qian Dajun and others at the headquarters on the 16th. Yu's mission is to await Zhang Xueliang. Also, Feng Yong arrived in Hankou on the 16th to await Zhang Xueliang (Sixteenth telegraphic special).

After arriving at the police station, he gave his name but said nothing else. The servant stated that he has a mental illness. (Hong Kong) The salvage ship "Taikoo," carrying 90 passengers, is currently in distress at sea due to the wind. A wireless message was received here this morning, stating that its location is approximately one hundred miles southwest of Dongsha. The British mine-laying cruiser "Adventure" (6,740 tons) has set sail to rescue it. (Seventeenth Reuters dispatch)

Thoughts on Chairman Chiang's Inspection Tour of Shaanxi and His Hopes for Shaanxi: An Address During an Expanded Memorial Week in Xi'an 96

Xi'an, 16th—Chairman Chiang delivered an address during the expanded memorial week for all circles on the 15th, titled "Thoughts on a Tour of Shaanxi and Hopes for Shaanxi." The original text is as follows:

Chairman Shao, Director Yang, fellow comrades, today I, your brother, have come to Xi'an to participate in this expanded memorial week, which is a truly rare opportunity. Therefore, I feel very happy and honored. Now, I would like to take this opportunity to share my personal thoughts after visiting Shaanxi and my hopes for all comrades and fellow citizens in Shaanxi. As everyone knows, Shaanxi Province, especially Chang'an, is the birthplace of Chinese culture and can also be said to be the cradle of the Chinese nation. Since Emperor Huangdi founded the nation, from the Zhou Dynasty through the Qin, Han, and Tang Dynasties, Chang'an has been the capital of China. During this era, the Chinese nation, in terms of both military prowess and culture, continuously developed and reached its peak from here. Therefore, not only should the people who live in this place recognize the glory and greatness of this national history and resolutely take on the great task of national rejuvenation as their own responsibility, but also visitors from afar, if they are citizens of the Republic of China, descendants of Emperor Huangdi, and members of the Chinese nation, cannot help but feel deep historical emotions and be inspired. Seeing such beautiful rivers and mountains and the many historical sites of past dynasties, and recalling the great achievements of our ancestors in building the country and developing the nation, one can understand that our Chinese nation has the greatest creative ability and the most brilliant civilized history. At the same time, recalling the current critical situation of our country's survival, one cannot help but feel overwhelmed by the contrast between the past and the present. Look at how great our ancestors were, and how glorious our history was. But now, internal and external troubles come one after another, and the country is in a dangerous state of survival. Not only are we unable to keep pace with other countries and survive independently in the world, but we cannot even achieve the status of a third-rate country. Instead, we are about to be ranked as a semi-colonial territory and face the danger of being destroyed at any time. What a shame! What a sorrow! But we are all descendants of the wise emperors and divine ancestors of past dynasties since Emperor Huangdi. Our ancestors had such great intelligence, such a great spirit, and such great achievements. Do we not have them? Can we not inherit the glorious history and great achievements of our ancestors? The great intelligence, spirit, and achievements of our ancestors have certainly been passed down to us. We believe that our intelligence, spirit, and achievements will certainly not be much worse than those of the ancients. We should be able to build on the past and create a great cause. However, why is our nation so weak now, and why is our country so dangerous? The biggest fundamental reason is that the general public has forgotten the greatness of our ancestors and the glory of our national history. They have forgotten the greatest intelligence, the noblest virtue, the most excellent culture, and the most precious spirit inherent in their own nation. They have even forgotten the great foundation left by their ancestors and such magnificent rivers and mountains. Therefore, they have lost the inherent soul of the country and the nation, cannot respect themselves, cannot have confidence, cannot strive for progress, and have allowed the status of the country and the nation to decline and become increasingly dangerous. Yet, the general public is still unaware and does not strive to become stronger and save themselves, so as to shoulder the great responsibility of saving the country and revitalizing it. Everyone must understand that a person relies entirely on having a spirit and a soul. If one loses the soul and has no spirit, that person will certainly not be able to survive. Even if they temporarily survive, they are like dead people, what is called walking corpses, lingering breaths. The same is true for a country and a nation. If a country loses its soul and has no spirit, it will certainly perish and will not be able to continue to survive. The reason why our country and nation are in such a critical and declining state is precisely because we have lost the inherent and fundamental spirit and the true soul of our nation. Because we have no spirit and have lost our soul, we are scolded as half-dead, half-alive citizens, a half-dead, half-alive country and nation. Our country is in danger and our people are humiliated to this extent. How can we face our ancestors? How can we even have the face to live in the world? How can we see that our country and nation have already lost their inherent soul? We do not need to go to other provinces to see. Just looking at the current situation in Shaanxi, the birthplace of Chinese culture, can prove it. As I just said, Shaanxi is the birthplace of Chinese culture and the cradle of the Chinese nation. Since the Duke of Zhou, King Wen, and King Wu, countless sages and heroes have emerged from this place, which has always been known as a land of culture and propriety. The Duke of Zhou's creation of rites and music made ancient Chinese politics, education, and culture complete and magnificent, which also began in Shaanxi. But when we look at Shaanxi now, the land is still the same, and the people are still the same, but the relics of the past and the old rites and music are gone. The inherent virtues of the Chinese nation, that is, the eight virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, harmony, and peace mentioned by the Generalissimo in the Three Principles of the People, as well as the fundamental spirit of China's founding for thousands of years, that is, the four dimensions of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame mentioned by Guan Zhong, are also neglected by many people. How can our country and nation not be in danger? Guan Zhong said that propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four dimensions of a country. If the four dimensions are not upheld, the country will perish. We recite these words and reflect on the past, and we cannot help but feel a chill down our spines. Now, if we want to save ourselves from danger and revitalize the nation, where should we start? The most important fundamental premise is that we must first restore the inherent soul of our country and nation. What is this soul? It is the eight virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, harmony, and peace that I just mentioned. Our ancestors were able to promote these eight virtues, so they were able to build such a great nation and country. Now, because we do not emphasize the eight virtues and have lost our soul, our country is in danger and our people are humiliated to this day. Therefore, to save ourselves from danger and revitalize the nation, we must prescribe the right medicine and restore this great soul. How can we achieve this goal? In other words, how can we restore, express, and complete the eight virtues? We must first practice the four dimensions of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, especially starting with the word "propriety." For example, when we hold a memorial week today, everyone salutes the flag of the Party and the country and the portrait of the Generalissimo. This is a kind of propriety. From this propriety, we can show that we believe in the Generalissimo, are loyal to the Party and the country, and are willing to sacrifice everything for the Generalissimo, for the Party, and for the country. With this sincere and respectful intention, we can completely restore and fully promote the eight virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, harmony, and peace, build a new country based on the Three Principles of the People, and revitalize our civilized and outstanding Chinese nation. The above is about the fundamental path for us to save ourselves from danger and revitalize the nation in the future, which lies in practicing the four dimensions and restoring the eight virtues. Now, I have one more point to add, that is, the practice of the four dimensions should start from daily life at any time and any place. That is, our food, clothing, housing, and transportation must all conform to propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. The main purpose of the New Life Movement is also here. Therefore, if we want to practice the four dimensions, restore the eight virtues, save ourselves from danger, and revitalize the nation, we must promote the New Life Movement and improve our lives according to the standards of the New Life. Our simple and unadorned lifestyle has always been the legacy of Shaanxi, and everyone can generally achieve it. What we should pay the most attention to in the future is to strive to achieve the four standards of tidiness, cleanliness, speed, and certainty. The basic condition for achieving these four standards is diligence. Only with diligence can we be tidy, only with diligence can we be clean, and only with diligence can we be fast and certain. King Wen never had leisure from sunrise to sunset, and the Duke of Zhou continued day and night, sitting and waiting for dawn. This is the best model left by our ancestors. In the heyday of the country and the nation, the ancients were still so diligent. Now, when the country and the nation are in a critical situation, if we want to survive and revitalize, we must be extraordinarily diligent. I hope that all comrades in Shaanxi must cultivate diligence and endurance, practice the New Life Movement, and take the lead in promoting the New Life Movement, so as to influence others from themselves, spread from Shaanxi Province to the whole country, and enable all compatriots in the country to practice the New Life Movement, practice propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. In this way, Shaanxi can shoulder the responsibility of revitalizing the nation, and be worthy of being the descendants of Emperor Huangdi and the followers of the Generalissimo. Everyone must remember that Shaanxi is the cradle of the Chinese nation and the birthplace of Chinese culture. Moreover, the people of Shaanxi have always been known for their chivalry, righteousness, and knowledge of propriety and shame. Since ancient times, Guanzhong has produced countless sages and heroes. Not only has there been no lack of people in history, but even recently, the legacy has not declined. Many revolutionary martyrs have struggled and sacrificed for the country, for the nation, and for the revolution. Therefore, Shaanxi, whether in terms of history, geography, culture, or politics, cannot be regarded as an ordinary province. It is the most important foundation of the country and the nation. Therefore, all comrades in Shaanxi, living in such an extraordinary place, must especially recognize the importance of their own position and the responsibilities they bear, and must especially strive to shoulder the mission of saving the country from danger and revitalizing the nation. In recent years, Shaanxi has made considerable progress in politics, military affairs, economy, and academics and culture. However, according to the current progress, it still cannot reach the expected standards and is not enough to shoulder the responsibility of revitalizing the nation. In the future, I hope that everyone will pay attention to the meaning of the four dimensions and the eight virtues that I have spoken about today, and strive to lay the foundation for the revolution and shoulder the responsibility of revitalizing the nation. In the past, King Wen, King Wu, the Duke of Zhou, Emperor Qin Shi Huang, Emperor Wu of Han, and Emperor Taizong of Tang all used Shaanxi as a foundation to build great countries and promote the prestige of the nation, which was rare in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. We are all descendants of our ancestors. The great intelligence, great spirit, and great foundation of our ancestors have been passed down to us. As long as we can recognize them clearly and can develop them, each of us can become King Wen, King Wu, the Duke of Zhou, Emperor Qin Shi Huang, Emperor Wu of Han, Emperor Taizong of Tang, etc. Although their careers were selfish to the emperors and are not suitable for today's modern times, their spirit of promoting national spirit and enhancing the history of China is a kind of spirit that we, as descendants, should be proud of, and everyone should have this kind of confidence in revitalizing the nation, and should not abandon themselves. Fellow comrades, especially the young people, must know that the current era environment in China is really the best opportunity that we can encounter in a thousand years to achieve great achievements and establish great careers. Whether from the historical, geographical, or cultural point of view, all kinds of conditions are complete. In particular, the current era environment can be said to be forcing us to become heroes and heroes who revitalize the nation. Now, as long as we can strive to become stronger and never give up, we will definitely be able to achieve the goal of revitalizing the nation and complete the mission of the era that we bear. This time I came to Xi'an, and I could not help but have infinite thoughts everywhere I touched the scene. At the same time, I also have infinite hopes for all comrades and fellow citizens in Shaanxi. Today, I took the opportunity of Memorial Week to report it briefly. I believe that everyone must have the same feelings, and will definitely be able to strive to fulfill everyone's responsibilities according to what I hope for everyone. The future of the country and the nation will definitely have unlimited light from now on. (Central News Agency)

October 17th Reuters Special Business Report 97

(Gold and Silver) ▲London Gold Price: The London gold price fell two and a half pence this morning, to 142 shillings and 7 pence.

▲London Silver Bar: This morning, the silver price fell sharply. Speculators engaged in profit-taking, leading to a market price drop of one penny. The spot price is 23 and 875/1000 pence, and the futures price is 24 pence. The closing trend is stable.

▲Bombay Silver Bar: The Bombay silver price fell five pounds. The spot price is 67 rupees and 5 annas, the November price is 67 rupees and 6 annas, and the December price is 67 rupees and 10 annas. The market situation is stable.

(Exchange Rates) ▲British-American: This morning, the London foreign exchange market had a psychological reaction because U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau claimed that the United States would continue to purchase silver. The British-American exchange rate opened at 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 34375/10000, which was 3125/10000 lower than yesterday's closing price for the American-British exchange rate. It then rebounded immediately. At 2 p.m., the price was 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 475/100, which was 13125/10000 higher than the opening price. Also, one U.S. dollar is equivalent to 4 shillings and 0509/10000 British pounds.

▲British-French: The opening price was 74 francs and 09 centimes, which was six pounds lower than yesterday. But by 2 p.m., it had risen 12 pounds, to 74 francs and 21 centimes.

▲American-British: The New York foreign exchange market opened this morning with a sharp rise in the pound, at 4 dollars and 95 cents, which was 125/100 higher than yesterday's closing price. But soon after, it fell 75/100, to 4 dollars and 94 and 25/100 cents. At 10:40 a.m., this price had not changed.

(Cotton and Wheat) ▲American Cotton: The cotton market was firmer due to good news from Washington. Demand was quite strong, so the opening price rose about three pounds. There was some hedging, but it was absorbed. The latest price is about four pounds higher than the opening price.

▲Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was closed today.

▲British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market rose slightly. At 1 p.m., the March futures price rose one pound, to 665.

▲British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market fell slightly this morning. At 1 p.m., the December futures price was 5 shillings, 3 and 125/1000 pence, a drop of 125/1000.

▲American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened at a price that was 125/1000 lower due to poor overseas telecommunications. However, the domestic situation was strong, and the market situation improved. The latest price is 25/100 higher than the opening price.

(Rubber) ▲London: The rubber market situation is stable. At noon, the transaction price for the January-March futures was 7 and 125/1000 pence, which is the same as yesterday's closing price.

▲New York: When the rubber market opened, the upward trend of yesterday still existed. The opening price was about eleven pounds higher than yesterday's closing price. It then rose another four pounds. However, the bulls took the opportunity to close out positions, and the market price had already fallen six pounds at the time of the dispatch.

(Securities) ▲New York: The sentiment in the New York securities market before the opening this morning was that securities would respond to construction news and believed that the authorities would focus on commercial recovery rather than social improvement events in the coming months. However, there was nothing exciting about the real estate news. Merchants may not dare to follow easily when securities prices rise. When the securities market opened this morning, the market situation was firm and stable, and trading was quite active. Although the amount of the rise was limited to single digits, the sentiment was more pleasant than before, and the upward trend seemed to be expanding slightly. Yu Xuezhong Arrives in Hankou 98

After Visiting Zhang Xueliang, He Will Go to Beijing

Yu Discusses the Latest Situation in North China

Hankou Correspondence: Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, needs to report to Chairman Chiang and President Wang regarding the post-war problems in the war zone. He left Tianjin for Ping after attending the opening ceremony of the North China Games on the 12th, transferred to a special train on the Pinghan Railway southward, arrived in Zhengzhou on the evening of the 13th, and stayed for two days. Chairman Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang happened to be going from Xi'an to Bian, so he came to Hankou from Zhengzhou on the 15th to pay his respects. At 6 p.m. on the 16th, he arrived at the Dazhimen Station in Hankou. The accompanying personnel were only Li Xigeng, Secretary of the Hebei Provincial Government, and Vice Adjutants Han and Mi. The military and political personnel here welcomed him warmly. After getting off the train, Yu stayed at the Yangtze River Hotel. When reporters sent their cards to visit, he was received and made a statement, saying that the security of Pingjin was very solid, and the war zone was also peaceful. However, since the Yutian Security Team incident and the Miyakoshi incident occurred one after another, the latent bandits began to stir. Fortunately, they have all been resolved peacefully. After Chairman Huang Yingbai returned to Ping and resumed his duties, progress has been made in the post-war negotiations in the war zone. At this plenary session of the Political Committee, it was decided to establish a war zone reorganization committee to be responsible for handling post-war matters. The outside world's claim that a war zone security office will be established is actually a misreporting of rumors. The handover of the counties within the Great Wall has been largely completed. Security is maintained by the security team. The handover of Dongling is currently under negotiation. Overall, the entire situation in North China is still optimistic. After the Changyuan breach, Sun Qingze, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, was removed from his post for ineffective protection. Due to the current flooding, the breach in the Yellow River cannot be blocked immediately. We can only first block the water flow to gradually reduce the breach. After the water recedes, we will make a fundamental defense plan. After I visit Deputy Commander Zhang in Hankou, I still plan to go to Beijing and then return to Tianjin via the Jinpu Railway, etc. (16th)

Yin Rugeng and Chayama Inspect the War Zone 99

First to Malanyu, Then to Dongling

Yutian Security Team Flees and Becomes Bandits

Tianjin Customs Establishes Xifengkou Branch Card at Panjiakou

Beiping Correspondence: Yin Rugeng, Administrative Inspector of the Ji-Mi District, accompanied by Chayama Kenjiro, Army Attaché of the Japanese Embassy, Watanabe, Naval Attaché, He Xiaoyi, the new magistrate of Zunhua County, Huang Zhongkai, the magistrate of Yutian County, and others, a total of seven people, departed in two cars and a truck at 6:30 a.m. yesterday to inspect Malanyu Dongling. At 8 a.m., they passed through Tongxian. A squad from the first company of the second regiment of the war zone security force accompanied them for protection. They arrived in Jixian at 2 p.m. and stayed briefly. He Xiaoyi and Huang Zhongkai got off the bus and went to their respective posts. At 3 p.m., they continued to move forward. They arrived in Malanyu at 7 p.m. on the same day. Yin resided at the Malanyu Office, and Chayama and others resided at the Japanese Army Regiment Headquarters. They went to Dongling for inspection together this afternoon. After the matter, Chayama and others transferred to Tangshan. According to Yin's pre-departure statement, the purpose of this trip is: (1) Many of the Dongling buildings and tombs have been damaged and occupied in the past due to poor management, which should be investigated; (2) More than 10,000 Banner people living in the Dongling Malanyu area are living in poverty. After investigating the actual situation, we will discuss relief measures; (3) Prepare all necessary procedures for the handover. It is planned to stay in Changdi for one day and then return to Ping. Recently, a part of the Japanese puppet troops originally stationed in Malanyu were transferred out. The Japanese Kwantung Army stationed in Chengde Special Service Agency dispatched more than 100 people to the village on the 13th from Rehe to Malanyu to assist in handling the handover of Dongling. After the two groups of bandits in Zunhua and Yutian were defeated, they gathered in the Dabishan area. After being attacked by the Japanese puppet troops on the Great Wall line, the bandits dispersed and fled to the five counties of Pinggu, Shunyi, Miyun, Zunhua, and Huairou. A group that fled to Huairou was driven away by the security team on the 14th and scattered again. The war zone security team is currently on strict alert.

The Jixian-Miyun Commissioner's Office in Ping received a telephone report from the Zunhua County Government at 7 p.m. today (16th) that Yin Rugeng, Commissioner of Jixian-Miyun, Chayama Kenjiro, Military Attaché of the Japanese Embassy, and others passed through Zunhua and arrived in Malanyu at 7 p.m. last night (15th). Yin rested at the local commissioner's office and then went to Xinglong County to stay. Chayama went to the Japanese military unit Yoshida's unit to inspect. This morning, Yoshida sent a team to escort Yin and Chayama to Dongling for inspection. They returned to Zunhua at 5:30 p.m. that evening. The group stayed at the Zunhua County Government and decided to go to Yutian tomorrow morning (17th) to inspect the scene of the Miyakoshi case. It is expected to return to Beiping in three or four days.

According to people from Zunhua, many of the current Yutian security team have fled and become bandits. The joint defense of the Fengrun, Zunhua, and Jixian militia is blocking them. It is estimated that the Fengrun defense line runs from the Shaliu River to the Jieshangkou, the Zunhua defense line runs from the Jieshangkou to Gongli, and the Jixian defense line runs from west of Gongli to Yanshangkou, with Gongli as the main camp. The magistrates of Fengrun, Zunhua, and Yutian are all stationed in "Gongli" to direct the defense. The Zunhua militia is paid 60 cents per person per day for food. If there are deaths, each person is paid 300 yuan, and if there are injuries, 100 yuan. All are from Zunhua County. The county people now have the mentality of "better to be broken jade than a whole tile" and are determined to destroy their families to relieve the disaster.

After the establishment of the Tianjin Customs Great Wall Five Pass Branch Cards, the Ministry of Finance, based on reports that smuggling was rampant at Panjiakou south of Xifengkou, ordered the Tianjin Customs to establish a Xifengkou Card Branch at that pass, limited to the 17th of this month. The Tianjin Customs has appointed Zhang Lianzhu as the director to prepare. He will prepare to establish an office tomorrow (17th). The announcement of the Beiping Office of the Tianjin Customs Great Wall Pass Branch Card Management Office is recorded as follows: "Inquiry Regarding the establishment of cards at various Great Wall passes, all Gubekou, Yiyuan, Lengkou, Xifengkou, and Jielingkou branch cards, the date of establishment, and the tax collection method have been announced by this Customs for your information. Now, according to the order of the Ministry of Finance, a branch office will be established at Panjiakou, which will be under the jurisdiction of the Xifengkou branch card. We hereby order you to comply. We have sent personnel to Panjiakou and prepared the branch office there. It will be established on October 17th and will start collecting taxes. The method is the same as that of the Great Wall branch cards. From now on, all goods passing through Panjiakou must go to the card office to comply with the regulations and verify them. Those who should pay taxes according to the Great Wall branch card tax collection method should also pay customs duties separately in accordance with the regulations. This announcement is hereby made to all Chinese and foreign merchants and people. This is the announcement. Supervisor Han Linsheng, Tax Commissioner Bos, Deputy Tax Commissioner Zhang Yongnian." (16th)

Recent Work of the Mongolian Political Council 100

Divided into two categories: Planning and Investigation

Japanese and Puppet Troops Prepare for Military Invasion of Mongolia

A dispatch from Beiping: After the central government decided to allocate funds monthly for the expenses of the Mongolian Autonomous Political Affairs Committee, all rumors were dispelled, and all misunderstandings were cleared away. Recently, there has been talk that the Mongolian Political Council will establish a representative office in Beiping to facilitate communication. De Wang, the Secretary-General of the council, sent Chen Shaowu as a representative to Nanjing and Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Jingwei. Chen returned to Beiping from Nanjing a few days ago and told visitors that the rumors about Mongolia were not true. He also praised Chiang, Wang, and other important figures for their concern for the Mongolian border. Chen is scheduled to leave Beiping for Bailingmiao tomorrow (the 17th) to report back. This reporter visited Chen today (the 16th) to inquire about the work of the Mongolian Political Council, and he stated the following:

According to Chen Shaowu, the work of the Mongolian Political Council was indeed in a state of semi-suspension in the past due to funding issues. However, the members and staff did not feel discouraged, and there were no disagreements. Their sincerity towards the central government was not affected. The rumors circulating outside are best refuted by the facts. Chen also said that he felt spiritually comforted after meeting with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Jingwei, which cannot be expressed in a few words. He has telegraphed De Wang about the details and will present Chairman Chiang's personal letter when he returns to the temple. Chiang gave detailed instructions on the Mongolian political measures, which the Mongolian Political Council will implement accordingly. As for the recent work of the Mongolian Political Council, it can be broadly divided into two categories: planning and investigation. The planning aspect is divided into education, industry, security, and civil administration. Because education in Mongolia is relatively backward, the first step is to promote production education and universal education. In terms of industry, because Mongolia is vast and transportation is inconvenient, all construction is affected. Therefore, the industrial plan focuses on transportation infrastructure. As for security, because the Mongolian border defense is weak, and Mongolians are skilled in horsemanship and archery, it is planned to recruit twenty Mongolians from each banner for equestrian training for a period of six months. After graduation, they will return to their original banner to be responsible for local defense. In terms of civil administration, all measures must start with investigation due to the religious ties of the Mongolian people. When Chen finally spoke about the funding issue of the council, he happily told the reporter that the central government has decided to allocate 30,000 yuan per month, which can be used for staff salaries and office expenses. As for construction costs, they will be discussed in the future.

A certain agency in Beiping received intelligence from Rehe this morning (the 16th) stating that the puppet organization intends to place the Ujimqin and Bairin banners under the jurisdiction of the puppet Xing'an Province in order to seize the Mongolian salt flats. The princes of the two banners, believing that the salt flats are of great importance to the livelihood of the Mongolian people, refused to comply. In late last month, they jointly led more than 20,000 Mongolian soldiers from the two banners and engaged in fierce clashes with the Japanese and puppet troops in Linxi County, shooting down four Japanese planes. The situation is serious. The Japanese and puppet troops are now concentrated on the highways around Tongliao, Kailu, Suidong, and Chifeng, preparing to conquer Mongolia by force. According to foreign sources, the Ujimqin and Bairin banners are the strongest among the leagues and banners of Inner Mongolia. They are currently in conflict with the Japanese and puppet troops and are in a stalemate. The future developments are worthy of attention. (Note: Linxi County is about 1,200 li from Chengde. Ujimqin is under the jurisdiction of the Xilingol League and is on the border of Chahar. Bairin is under the jurisdiction of the Josutu League and is within Rehe.) (16th)

Jiading: Gu Shaochuan Plans to Establish a Cotton Mill 101

Gu Shaochuan, the envoy to France and a native of this county, in order to help the common people of his hometown, has joined with Gu Jisheng, Tao Jiyuan, and other prominent merchants from this county who reside in Shanghai to raise capital and establish a cotton mill in this county. They have already selected a site next to the Lianqi River on the Xihu Road outside the West Gate and have submitted a request to the county government for permission to purchase land from the people. They are actively proceeding with the project.

Cannon Shells Found Behind the Shrine 102

During a house cleaning at the Yangwang Temple in Waigang a few days ago, four 75mm flat-trajectory cannon shells, two field artillery shell heads, two mortar shells, four grenades with handles, four grenades without handles, and two steel helmets were found in the jumbled bricks behind the shrine. They are believed to have been hidden by the National Revolutionary Army during the January 28th Incident. They have been sent to the town's public education center for public display.

Wuxi: Butchers Strike and Petition 103

The slaughter tax for the meat industry in the urban area was previously 69.3 yuan per day. After Shou Hezhang (i.e., Mu Jun) contracted it, the amount was increased, and he negotiated with the meat merchants to increase it by 10 yuan per day. The meat merchants refused. Later, the county chamber of commerce mediated and suggested an increase of 5 yuan. The meat merchants only agreed to 4.2 yuan, which was not resolved. The meat merchants then voluntarily agreed to be taxed item by item, which took effect on the 16th. The slaughter tax collection office then dispatched a large number of staff to the shops to collect the tax item by item. For some reason, the collection office sent Lu Guangchang, Ji Bingzhang, Lu Gaojian, Guo Zhiyuan, Hu Abing of Xin Sanzhen, and Zhou Xusheng of Hongyishun to the Public Security Bureau for detention. At 4:00 p.m. that afternoon, the county chamber of commerce mediated again, but failed to resolve the issue. This aroused the resentment of the entire meat industry, and they all went on strike on the 17th. Yesterday morning, more than 300 people appointed Yao Zhongqing, Lian Jianshu, Zhu Xifan, Xu Zhuyou, Ren Shouqin, Wang Yulin, and Shao Tinglan as representatives to petition the county party headquarters, requesting two things: (1) Please order the county Public Security Bureau to immediately release the detained colleagues and ensure that similar incidents do not occur again. (2) Since taxes are already being collected item by item, do not use this as an excuse to harass them. As for the issue of stamping pig carcasses, which affects business and public health, please change it to stamping the head. Commissioner Xu Chizi came out to meet them and promised to discuss the four detained meat merchants with the county government and order the Public Security Bureau to release them. The issue of item-by-item stamping should be mediated by the county chamber of commerce. The petition representatives then went to the county government to petition, and County Magistrate Yan personally met them and advised them to resume business immediately to avoid losses. Since the dispute is being mediated by the chamber of commerce, the chamber of commerce should be responsible for resolving it. There is no problem with the request to release the four detained colleagues. At 12:00 noon, they went to the county chamber of commerce to petition and submitted a letter requesting assistance. Zou Tongyi and Li Bosen met with them and promised to forward the original letter, but they said that the chamber of commerce could not mediate the dispute between the meat merchants and the tax office because the opinions of both sides were in conflict, making mediation difficult and creating a stalemate. The petition representatives left because their petition was unsuccessful. It is feared that this dispute will escalate.

Sudden Change to Severe Cold Weather 104

The weather this summer was hot and dry, and since autumn, after the lunar Mid-Autumn Festival, it was still exceptionally muggy. People were still sweating in single-layer clothing. Unexpectedly, in the past two days, the weather has suddenly turned severely cold, with the Fahrenheit thermometer dropping to 49 degrees. People feel cold even in cotton-padded clothing. Fortunately, the weather is clear, and it warms up slightly in the afternoon. However, because of this drastic change in temperature, throat ailments are very prevalent in the city.

Owner of a South Goods Store Commits Suicide in Despair 105

Zhang Yaoshan, the 40-year-old owner of the Xinda South Goods Store in Xicang Bridge under the shed outside the West Gate, has a mother, a wife, a son, and two daughters. The children are all young. When Zhang first opened the south goods store, business was good. Recently, due to the economic downturn, business plummeted, leading to financial difficulties and heavy debt. In addition, Zhang was addicted to gambling and often lost, which made things even more difficult. He became weary of life and secretly took many sleeping pills the day before yesterday morning. Around 7:00 p.m. that evening, the poison took effect, causing vomiting. His wife discovered it and immediately called Dr. Hong Chun for treatment. However, the poisoning was too deep, and there was no hope of recovery. He died at 8:30 a.m. yesterday, which is very tragic.

Wu County has suffered severe drought this year, and many fields in various townships have yielded no harvest. The county government had already dispatched officials to conduct preliminary surveys of the affected fields, compile a register, and submit a report. After contacting the county government, they dispatched Lu Zezhi, the head of the Second Section, to accompany them on a re-survey. The three-hall committee and the county committee hired a boat today (the 17th) to go to Xiangxia Yiqiao and other places to investigate, and then to other townships, which will take about ten days to complete.

Buddhist scholar Master Taixu, invited by the Huiyin Temple in Dantu Town, arrived in Zhenjiang from Nanjing at around 6:00 p.m. yesterday to transmit precepts and lecture on sutras at the temple. After Master Taixu got off the train, he greeted everyone with clasped hands and boarded a car directly to the Chao'an Temple in Xiaomatou, where he rested. He himself also wanted to travel to Zhenjiang, which has many famous mountains and ancient temples. He will go to Dantu to lecture on the sutras tomorrow (i.e., this morning). After that, he plans to return to his hometown for a short stay. It is said that Xue Song, the abbot of Chao'an Temple, and Customs Commissioner Zhang have jointly invited Lu Xiaobo and other prominent figures in the Zhenjiang business community to invite Taixu to give public lectures in the province for a few days after he finishes lecturing at Huiyin Temple in order to promote the true essence of Buddhism.

In the coastal areas of Tongru in northern Jiangsu, sea bandits are rampantly invading, robbing, and kidnapping people. Chen Hai, an apprentice at a Chen surname shoe store in the west of the city, was brutally murdered while going out to relieve himself at night. His body was found in the fields of a Zhou surname.
