Education News

Returned Northeast Traveler Discusses the Implementation of Enslavement Education in the Puppet State 193

▲Party ideology materials are strictly prohibited in the curriculum.

▲Schools have decreased compared to before, and a large number of young people are out of school.

Since the September 18th Incident, our compatriots in the Northeast have suffered deeply under the oppression of the puppet government in the puppet state. The Ministry of Culture and Education of the puppet state implemented enslavement education to numb the will of young people. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency met Mr. Wang, who had returned from the Northeast, at his residence and discussed the situation of education in the puppet state.

(Party Ideology Materials are Prohibited) According to the discussion, the educational policy of the Ministry of Culture and Education of the puppet state, in name, takes emphasizing the Kingly Way and advocating benevolence and righteousness as its banner. It orders schools in various provinces to add the Four Books and the Classic of Filial Piety to the curriculum. In reality, it goes against this. The Ministry of Culture and Education has also issued an order that all materials related to party ideology are strictly prohibited and will be charged with anti-imperialism." The educational departments of Fengtian Province and the South Manchurian Educational Society are currently editing various textbooks, which will then be reviewed and published by the Ministry of Culture and Education. The content is self-evident.

(Reduced Schools and Youth Out of School) The number of schools in the Northeast has now decreased. Before the September 18th Incident, Liaoning Province had 10,350 schools, now only 6,885. Jilin Province had 1,286 schools, now only 449. Heilongjiang Province had 600 schools, now only 432. Xing'an Province had 44 schools, now only 34. The Northeast Special District had 152 schools, now only 143. Rehe had 878 schools, now only 5. Therefore, more than 95% of the youth in the Northeast are out of school.

(Larger Number of Students Studying in Japan) Most schools require Japanese as a compulsory subject, widely establishing Japanese language training centers and encouraging study in Japan. Therefore, in recent years, the puppet state has 107 government-funded students studying in Japan and 109 self-funded students, while only 15 government-funded students and 6 self-funded students are studying in Europe. School fees have increased. Before the September 18th Incident, primary schools cost 7 yuan per year, but now they have increased to 32 yuan per year. There is currently no national university. Recently, someone suggested turning Northeastern University and Jilin University into national universities. The puppet state also collected and reorganized the Wensu Pavilion Siku Quanshu and the collections of Northeastern University and Zhang Xueliang, turning Zhang's private residence into a national library.

(Organizing Youth Groups to Visit Japan) In terms of sports, the puppet state, in addition to holding National Day sports meets last year and this year, orders schools to select and organize student youth groups. The organization is similar to the Boy Scouts. The puppet army is guided and trained by the Japanese, and each province selects youth groups to visit Japan. Their every move is completely a puppet behavior.

A Personal View on Implementing Production Education (5) 197

▲Speech by Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan at the Members' Meeting of the Third District Education Association

To make primary and secondary school education break away from the whirlpool of consumption and profit-sharing and transform into an activity of production work, it is natural to reform teaching materials, curriculum, etc., but what is especially important is to have a general enthusiastic, striving, and skilled teaching staff. Speaking of the distribution of the curriculum, although there are now standards set by the ministry, these curriculum standards may not be entirely suitable for practical use or ideal, because the gentlemen who draft and review the curriculum standards may not be experts in researching and compiling the curriculum, but rather experts in a certain subject. Experts in a certain subject often believe that the subject they are good at teaching is the most important, so they request a lot of time for the subject and allocate a lot of time. This is human nature. Therefore, to reform the distribution of the curriculum, we cannot rely solely on a few subject experts who draft and review the curriculum, but rather on teachers in primary and secondary schools who are enthusiastic about research. They regard education as a lifelong career, a career that has a very important relationship with the country and the nation. While studying the selection of teaching materials, they also study the distribution of the curriculum. By pooling their ideas, they will definitely be able to come up with a good reform plan. To be honest, if the central school teachers in Shanghai can truly enthusiastically study the curriculum and teaching materials for the implementation of production education, and one day have a very good plan, it can naturally be used as a reference for the whole country and as a model for the whole country. Why is that? Many people who run education and study normal schools in the interior often come to Shanghai to inspect and "sightsee." If Shanghai does not have new things and good methods to experiment with for people to observe and learn from, and it is still the same as before, always imitating the old, then what glory do we have? Wouldn't it become "seeing but not glorious?" However, this kind of experimentation with new methods and creation of new things in order to make a contribution is really a difficult task. On the one hand, you have to teach students, and on the other hand, you have to bury yourself in research, and then you can transform teaching materials and curriculum onto the great road of production. Surely many people will say, "We are busy from morning to night now teaching, grading homework, and practicing workbooks. To ask us to do research again is tantamount to taking our lives." But we must think of the trend of international oppression and the danger of the national situation, and we must actively carry out the work. At the same time, we must think that the living environment of primary and secondary school teachers in Shanghai is much better than that of their counterparts in other inland areas. For example, in bandit areas, for example, in disaster areas, this is not to be had. Therefore, we should do our best.

Today, by taking advantage of the opportunity of the Third District Education Association's meeting, I can contribute my recent thoughts on education. I cannot but thank the Third District Education Association for giving me this opportunity. I hope that everyone will work together to set a basic principle for reforming education, and everyone will work together to collect materials, research plans, and act as pioneers in reforming education. Only in this way can Shanghai's education be brought back to life. I believe that if Shanghai's education can be brought back to life, it can become popular throughout the country, because everyone is looking to Shanghai for its appearance. As long as Shanghai changes direction, the inland will follow suit. It can almost be said that our future policy is the new trend of primary and secondary school education throughout the country. We should, under the guidance of the Ministry of Education's emphasis on production education, strive for practical facilities and work. The Ministry of Education sees that what the whole country needs is the reform of teaching materials and curriculum, and it will definitely adopt and find ways to meet the needs of the whole country. I hope that you will work hard for production education. (End)

Lu Province Educational Supervisor Permanently Stationed in Districts 198

▲ Trial Implementation of Stationing Inspection Method to Start in Qingzhou and Jining Districts

(Jinan Quick News) The Shandong Provincial Department of Education, considering that in the past, educational supervisors inspected the educational administrative conditions of all districts on a quarterly basis, dividing the province into twelve districts. This was limited by time and made it difficult to fulfill the responsibility of supervision, feeling that it was not perfect. Now, in order to improve supervision efficiency, a pioneering initiative in the national education field is being implemented: a method of permanently stationing educational supervisors in districts for inspection. It has now been decided to first send educational supervisor Wu Hongwang to Qingzhou (Ninth District) and Feng Guangrong to Jining (Third District) for the first year of trial implementation. In the second year, this will be extended to six districts, and in the third year, it will cover all twelve districts in the province. The goal is to make this three-year trial a pioneering undertaking in the education field. On the 16th of this month, Supervisors Wu and Feng will depart simultaneously to begin the trial implementation. It is reported that the method of stationing supervisors in districts has been drafted. As for the educational supervisor inspections this autumn, they will still be carried out as usual, with supervisors of all districts scheduled to depart on the 16th, completing the inspections within two months. Inspections of schools at all levels in Jinan City have now been completed. The details of the method of stationing supervisors in districts are disclosed below:

The stationed district educational supervisor should perform the following duties: (1) General inspection; (2) Special inspection; (3) Matters assigned by the Department's order. Whenever a stationed district supervisor finishes inspecting the education of a county, they should separately convene meetings of the county's educational administrative personnel and teachers and staff of all levels of schools to study improvement matters and report them to the Department for verification and handling. Inspection reports of provincial schools should be submitted separately. When the entire district's education inspection is completed, a suitable location should be selected to convene a meeting of the heads of the Fifth Section or county supervisors of each county to discuss common areas for improvement in the district and submit the discussion conclusions to the Department for verification and handling. At the same time, special inspections should be carried out in counties with better performance in the entire district. Special attention should also be paid to the following three matters: (1) Consolidation of county education funds; (2) Improvement of education administrative efficiency; (3) Improvement of various education undertakings. If there are special circumstances in each county that affect the progress of education, or if a certain type of education is particularly backward, or if the implementation of a certain type of education is not suitable for local needs, or if there are special obstacles encountered in education, special inspections should be carried out.

The Statistics Committee of the Hubei Provincial Government recently compiled statistics on the current state of education in Hubei Province. Excerpts of the most important information are recorded below:

A. Schools at all levels in Hubei Province: (1) Elementary schools: 2,587 schools, with 123,616 male students and 36,054 female students, and 6,467 male and female teachers and staff, with an annual expenditure of 2,729,118 yuan. (2) Secondary schools: 76 schools, with 12,697 male students and 3,725 female students, and 2,058 male and female teachers and staff, with an annual expenditure of 1,472,004 yuan. (3) Higher education institutions: 5 institutions, with 720 male students and 149 female students, and 169 male and female teachers and staff, with an annual expenditure of 514,116 yuan. (The above includes provincial, municipal, county, and private schools at all levels. Elementary schools include kindergartens, junior elementary schools, and complete elementary schools. Secondary schools include middle schools, vocational schools, and normal schools. Higher education institutions include vocational colleges and universities.)

B. Private schools at all levels in the Hubei provincial capital and Hankou City: (1) Elementary schools: 75 schools, 288 classes, with 9,749 male and female students, and 587 teachers and staff, with a monthly expenditure of 19,772 yuan. (2) Secondary schools: 30 schools, 209 classes, with 5,259 male and female students, and 774 teachers and staff, with a monthly expenditure of 78,056 yuan. (3) Vocational schools: 1 school, 3 classes, with 59 students and 11 teachers and staff, with a monthly expenditure of 100 yuan. (4) Specialized schools: 2 schools, 8 classes, with 81 male and female students, and 34 teachers and staff, with a monthly expenditure of 5,092 yuan. (5) Universities: 2 schools, 40 classes, with 661 students and 103 teachers and staff, with a monthly expenditure of 32,849 yuan. (The above schools in the provincial capital refer to private schools at all levels within the jurisdiction of the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital, Wuchang and Hanyang areas.)

C. An analysis of provincial and municipal schools at all levels in Hubei Province. When kindergartens, junior elementary schools, complete elementary schools, middle schools, vocational schools, normal schools, and vocational colleges are all totaled, the provincial schools have 119 schools, 503 classes, 22,971 students, 1,735 teachers and staff, and a monthly expenditure of 134,438 yuan. The municipal schools have 62 schools, 242 classes, 12,235 students, 581 teachers and staff, and a monthly expenditure of 36,673 yuan.

D. An analysis of public and private schools at all levels in Hubei counties. When kindergartens, junior elementary schools, complete elementary schools, and vocational schools are all totaled, the public schools have 1,943 schools, 85,404 male students, 18,400 female students, 3,717 teachers and staff, and an annual expenditure of 953,651 yuan. The private schools have 434 schools, 16,360 male students, 4,534 female students, 1,152 teachers and staff, and an annual expenditure of 263,375 yuan. (Public schools refer to county-level and district-level schools. The annual expenditures of public kindergartens and vocational schools are not included because they were not reported.)

Zhou Feicheng and others elected as city representatives for the Seventh District

Tang Tianen and others elected as city representatives for the Ninth District

▲ Seventh District The Seventh District Education Association of this city held a general assembly of members at the Seventh District Party Headquarters yesterday morning. 104 members attended. Yu Zhongbiao from the City Party Headquarters, Nie Haifan from the City Education Bureau, and Xu Zeyi from the City Education Association attended to provide guidance. After the meeting, the chairman first gave a report, followed by speeches from Yu Zhongbiao, representing the City Party Headquarters, and Xu Zeyi, representing the City Education Association. Then the election was held. As a result of the ballot count, Zhou Feicheng, Xu Zeyi, Wu Chuijiu, and Wu Zhao were elected as representatives to the city. Diao Qing'en, Yan Zhengqing, Wang Wujun, Zhang Zhongmian, and Li Baozhen were elected as executive members. Zhou Yixiu and Cha Susheng were elected as alternate executive members. Then, proposals were passed: (1) In order to strengthen the organization of the Education Association, should the District Education Association adopt the current regulations allowing for a representative assembly, and should the branch be the basic organization? It is proposed that this be forwarded to the central government through the superior authorities to amend the law. The decision was made to forward it to the City Education Association. (2) This city has a dense population and high housing costs, making it difficult to obtain large school buildings. The current elementary school staffing is uneconomical. Should the City Education Bureau be petitioned to try the Gary Plan? The decision was made to forward it to the Education Bureau. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

▲ Ninth District The Ninth District Education Association of this city also held a general assembly of members yesterday at the Municipal Longhua Elementary School. Wang Longzhang, representing the City Party Headquarters, Nie Haifan from the City Education Bureau, Huang Zaoxiong from the City Education Association, and more than 60 members attended. Wu Rugui, Mei Hongquan, and Hu Wufeng served as the presidium. First, the chairman gave a report, followed by speeches from Wang Longzhang, Huang Zaoxiong, and others. Then an election was held. As a result, Tang Tianen, Mei Hongquan, Wu Rugui, and Zong Xiaojie were elected as city representatives. Many proposals were discussed at the end, and the meeting was then adjourned.

Dental Protection Association Offers Preferential Treatment to Students 202

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to schools at all levels in this city, stating that in accordance with a public letter previously approved by the Health Bureau, due to the increasingly difficult economic situation this year, all school health work will be temporarily reduced in scope, and all dental clinics will be temporarily suspended, etc. This bureau has already issued orders for notification. Regarding student dental correction matters, in addition to following the previous order to seek treatment at the Children's Dental Hospital of the Family Industrial Cooperative, it has now been negotiated with the China Dental Protection Association to offer preferential treatment for treatment. The fees are as follows: elementary school students: tooth extraction, 20 cents per tooth; filling, 40 cents per tooth; teeth cleaning, 50 cents. Students above the middle school level will be charged double. However, all elementary and middle school students will be charged a registration fee of 10 cents each, and dental examinations will be free of charge. Fillings will be charged at half the ordinary consultation fee. Treatment hours are from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM daily, from Monday to Saturday. The location is on the third floor of No. 47 Ningbo Road, Jiangxi Road intersection (opposite the Shanghai Bank). However, students from each school should present a health examination card and a dental treatment card, or a formal letter from the school, to seek treatment. In addition, in order to ensure dental health, student groups or individual students may join the association as members and are allowed to pay half the membership fee. Membership regulations can be obtained directly from the association. This order is issued for notification.

Change of Principal at Qiaoguang Middle School 207

Former Principal Qiu Hanping Returns to the Position

Qiaoguang Middle School in this city was founded by Qiu Hanping, Ma Canhan, and others in 1931. Qiu served as principal and Ma as vice principal. After more than a year of operation, the school was located in Nanyuan, Xinzha Road, and had hundreds of students, mostly overseas Chinese children. Later, Qiu Hanping resigned as principal due to his law practice and his studies at Soochow and Jinan Universities, which he could not manage at the same time. Ma Canhan took over, and it has been two years since then. Now, Mr. Ma has resigned from the board of directors due to illness. After deliberation by the directors, it was decided that the former principal, Qiu Hanping, should return to the position, so that he can easily get back into the swing of things and the school's affairs can be easily developed. It is said that Qiu Hanping, after being strongly urged by the directors, will arrive at the school to take charge in the near future.

Sports News

American Elite Track and Field Athletes Pass Through Shanghai, Will Perform Early Next Month 209

▲ A Group of Ten Arrived in Port at 6:00 AM Yesterday

▲ Will Tour the City and Depart for the Philippines on the Original Ship on the Same Day

A group of American elite track and field athletes performed excellently in Japan and were very popular. This time, at the invitation of the Philippines, they took the Pacific Company's General Pershing to go there. The ship arrived in Shanghai at 6:00 AM yesterday. The athletes went ashore to visit. They will take the original ship to depart for the Philippines at 4:00 PM. They will return to the country on the 22nd of next month. When passing through Shanghai, they will make a public performance. A reporter from the Shenshi News Agency specifically interviewed and recorded the details as follows.

▲ Arrived in Port at 6:00 AM Welcoming Personnel The General Pershing arrived at the port at about 6:00 AM yesterday morning. Sports organizations in Shanghai, such as the Westerners' YMCA, Taping Nautical YMCA, Hall & Holme School, and athletes' friends, all went on board to welcome them.

▲ Tour the City and Have Lunch at the Huizhong Hotel At about 8:00 AM, they went to the Nautical YMCA for a short rest. Under the leadership of Taping and Hall, they took three cars to tour the city center, Shen Garden, Hall & Holme School, Chenghuang Temple, and other places, and had lunch at the Huizhong Hotel.

▲ A Group of Ten, Eight Men and Two Women The athletes in this trip include Kevin Han, Clara Metcalf, Dunn, Thompson, Antenson, Huboster, Green, and others, totaling eight people, and two female family members. Other athletes returned to the United States earlier after completing their competitions in Japan.

▲ Sports Talents Full of Energy The athletes are all strong and full of energy. They have all achieved considerable results in the World Games and are talents in the contemporary sports world, such as Metcalf's sprint, Kevin Han and Green's middle distance, Thompson's pole vault, and Dunn's two irons.

▲ Athletes Talk About Their Impressions According to athlete Kevin Han and others' answers to questions from the Shenshi News Agency reporter, although the time in Shanghai was short, they traveled all over Shanghai and felt that the atmosphere was booming and had a good impression. The reporter then asked what opinions they had on Chinese sports. According to the answer, they were not very familiar with it and were not convenient to give a hasty criticism.

▲ Departed at 4:00 PM and Will Return Next Month The athletes returned to the ship one after another at about 3:00 PM in the afternoon. Friends went to bid farewell. The Pershing set sail at 4:05 PM. After performing in the Philippines, it was decided to come to Shanghai on the 22nd of next month. The performance issue, which was noisy, has been confirmed and will be held in Shen Garden in early next month.

Chu Minyi Talks About the North China Games 212

Chu Minyi arrived in Beijing at 8:00 AM on the 16th by the Pingpu Express train and immediately went to the Executive Yuan to attend a meeting. According to Chu's words to reporters, this time representing the Executive Yuan to Tianjin to participate in the North China Games, the round trip took more than ten days. The impression gained was very good. This North China Games was organized by the Hebei Provincial Government and the Tianjin Municipal Government, with a total cost of 460,000 yuan. 360,000 yuan was used to build the venue, and the remaining 100,000 yuan was used to entertain athletes from various places and conference staff. The venue construction is excellent, especially the opening of the entrance is appropriate, so during the conference, there was no crowding when the audience entered. The order was good. The results of the track and field competitions were also particularly advanced, breaking many national and North China records. The spirit and morals of the athletes from all over the world were especially good. There were no disputes during the several days of the meeting. Since the September 18th Incident, the morale of the people in North China has been declining. This time, young people from all over the world gathered in Tianjin and competed fiercely. The people have been greatly encouraged by this, showing a lot of vitality, which is a very meaningful event.

Chu Minyi telegraphed Yu Xuezhong, Zhang Boling, Wang Tao, and others on the 16th to thank them for their hospitality in Tianjin.

Jiangsu-Shanghai Sports School Joint Meeting 213

▲ Request the Ministry of Education to Postpone This Year's Unified Examination

▲ Track and Field Competition to Be Held in Shanghai on November 17th

The third meeting of the Jiangsu-Shanghai Sports School Joint Association was held at 3:00 PM on the 14th at the Chenglie Sports Normal School in Zhujiazhuang, Suzhou. Attendees included Huang Binsheng and Li Shao from Zhongshan Vocational School, (Ye Guanghui representing) Chinese Women's Sports Teacher School, Yu Ziyu (Wen Huaiyu representing) Southeast Women's Sports Teacher School, Lu Lihua from Liangjiang Women's Sports Teacher School, Zhu Songsun and Yang Tujian from Chenglie Sports Teacher School. East Asia Vocational School was absent. Zhu Songsun was the chairman, and Chen Dangshi was the recorder. The discussion items were as follows: (1) Request the Ministry of Education to postpone the graduation unified examination during this year's winter vacation. It was decided that the association would list the reasons and submit a document to the Ministry of Education requesting the postponement of the unified examination during this year's winter vacation. If a unified examination is required, the examination subjects should be changed. (2) How should the examination subjects be revised and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval? It was decided to list the reasons and request that the citizenship test be changed to the Party Principles test, and that the four subjects of history, geography, physics, and chemistry be exempted from the test, and that the following academic subjects be added: 1. Anatomy, 2. Physiology, 3. Ball sports, 4. Track and field sports, men's skillful sports, 5. Women's rhythmic activities. (3) Request the Ministry of Education to appoint teachers from various sports schools as examiners before the graduation unified examination. The decision was: Rejected. (4) Among the textbooks for each subject decided by the previous meeting, there are private works that have not been formally published and distributed, and there is no way to purchase them. How should this be remedied? The decision was: each school will temporarily choose its own textbooks, and the association will formulate a textbook survey form, distribute it to each school, and send it back to the association for collection and listing this month. Each school will submit various textbooks, and the teachers in charge will review and sign their opinions and submit them to the next conference to decide on a good version and adopt it uniformly. At present, teachers in each school should collect more materials in addition to the selected textbooks in order to facilitate students' participation in the unified examination. (5) The request to change the course of study issued by the ministry, which was decided at the previous meeting of the association, has already been sent. Should it be urged again to approve it before this year's winter vacation? The decision was reserved. (6) Each school in the association should add affiliated elementary and middle schools (or practical elementary schools) to facilitate internships and trial teaching. The decision was: Each school will handle it according to the situation. C. Provisional motions: (1) In the future, all correspondence from the association should be registered and mailed to avoid loss. The decision was: Passed. (2) All schools in the association should jointly hold various competitions. The decision was: Passed. The competitions will be held in Suzhou and Shanghai in turn. This semester, a track and field competition will be held first, scheduled for November 17th in Shanghai. The date of the next competition item will be decided at a temporary meeting after the track and field competition. The competition rules will be determined separately.

Hangzhou Art School Volleyball Team's Third Match 215

▲ Tied 2-2 with Shanghai University

丨 Game Stopped Due to Darkness 丨

丨 Today's Match Against Jiaotong University 丨

The Hangzhou Art School volleyball team has been winning consecutively in Shanghai against Dongya and Datong, as reported previously. Yesterday, they met the Shanghai champion, Shanghai University, and it was expected to be a heated match. However, the results exceeded expectations. This year, besides veteran players, Hangzhou Art School has added two Zhaos and one Huang. The skills of each player and the team's overall coordination have made remarkable progress. At 4 PM, the Shanghai University court was packed with spectators. The match began at 4 PM, with Liu Xuesong of Shanghai University as the referee. The competition was immediately filled with highlights. Veteran players from Shanghai University, such as Lu Kangyuan, who had attended the Far Eastern Games, repeatedly used sharp spikes. However, the front row of Hangzhou Art School was like an impenetrable copper wall. Moreover, Guan Qinghua scored points with cold shots, leading to a stalemate in the score. Later, the two Zhao players from Hangzhou Art School took the lead in spiking and scoring. However, they were repeatedly penalized, resulting in a tie of 20-20. Subsequently, both sides fought hard, making the game even more exciting than before. The third row of Hangzhou Art School, Chen, Zhou, and Huang, repeatedly saved dangerous balls. As a result, the scorekeeper recorded 26-24, with Hangzhou Art School winning the first set. At the beginning of the second set, Shanghai University vowed to counterattack, and Hangzhou Art School did not show any weakness. The score remained within one or two points. In the end, Shanghai University won with a score of 23-21. At the beginning of the third set, Hangzhou Art School gained the right to switch sides after achieving a score of 11-1. Shanghai University worked hard to attack, eventually entering a fierce battle situation at 20-20. The fans cheered wildly. However, Hangzhou Art School, remaining calm, won the third set with a score of 24-22. At the beginning of the fourth set, it was already dark, and both sides had entered a chaotic situation. The Shanghai University cheerleading squad shouted loudly, shaking the ground. Hangzhou Art School, due to its disadvantage in location, lost with a score of 18-21 to Shanghai University. By this time, the lights of thousands of homes were lit, and the game was stopped at a 2-2 tie. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

▲ Hangzhou Art School Team: Zhao Yunxiu, Zeng Xinquan, Wu Yisun, Huang Jinfen, Zhao Lianwu, Guan Qinghua, Wu Junyao, Zhu Ruji, Zhou Qingquan, Chen Guanyou, Huang Rongfa.

▲ Shanghai University Team: Yu Huiji, Huang Jiajun, Xu Senlin, Lu Kangyuan, Li Shufen, Zou Guoxiong, Li Jinliang, Wang Chongji, Chen Jacao, Ruan Shuyiao.

Free Talk

A Few Dissents on the Form and Legacy of Art 218

— Ye

In her article "The Form and Legacy of Art," Ms. Xin Ren treats the form of art as the artist's "Sety". She believes that "the primary task of the artist is to extract the content of art from reality, and then use their unique talent to process it artistically. In this process, the artist's greatest effort lies in finding a form that corresponds to the content and can increase the impact of the content. The artist's unique style is used to express the realities they have captured." This point easily leads to the misunderstanding that it is not the content that determines the form, but the writer's style during the process of artistically processing the captured realistic materials. The figurative expression of reality (the essence of phenomena, the phenomenal essence) is undoubtedly a process through the writer's consciousness, that is, it is expressed in the writer's consciousness. But this also involves the artist's skills and the dynamic expression methods, i.e., the role of the form that "increases the impact of the content." Therefore, we can see that the artist's artistic expression form is presented here as something secondary. The primary thing in the artist's artistic production process is the artist's attitude towards reality, i.e., the method or perspective the artist uses when extracting the content of art from concrete, objective reality, and how this material is expressed. If the writer is a strict realist, then the material they extract from reality and the form in which they express it must also be realistic. If a writer extracts a certain essential cross-section from reality, then when the artist processes it artistically, that is, expresses it figuratively, this "how" of expression has an inseparable, lawful relationship with the essential cross-section of the reality being captured. It is not determined by the artist's "whim," otherwise, the artist will fall into the danger of distorting reality or not faithfully expressing it. Overly emphasizing the uniqueness of the writer's style has the same result.

"The "permanence" of works of art is because they contain concrete (figurative) typical facts and characters rooted in reality. And these things are expressed by the artist in a comprehensive form..." The evaluation of the social value of art is based on translating it from artistic expression into sociological expression, and determining its sociological equivalence. But this is only one part of the work on the issue of legacy. The main work here focuses on the form of classical art, i.e., the question of "how to express it." This is precisely the question of creative methods, i.e., how they can provide us with suggestions for creative methods in some areas, that is, the question of re-examining, correctly understanding, "and obtaining new techniques and new creative methods from it," rather than imitating the style of a certain writer.

"We know that artists like Shakespeare, Balzac, Goethe, and Tolstoy had consciousnesses that went against history. However, because they constantly sought out reality, the process of practice gradually eroded and dissolved their worldview..." Like Mr. Ren Baige, Mr. Xin Ren attributes the solution to the contradiction between Balzac, Tolstoy, and others' worldview and creative methods to the results of these writers' creative practice. However, in reality, I think it is more due to social changes. Balzac and Tolstoy's consciousness went against history. Because of this, they never fully grasped the unity of worldview and creative method, and this is precisely what restricted their development and manifested in the wavering consciousness in their works. However, this still does not prevent them from becoming realists.

Mr. Xin Ren believes that "the "permanence" of works of art is because they contain concrete (figurative) typical facts and characters rooted in reality." This is precisely to say whether the reality embodied in works of art has historicity and sociality. It uses concrete images to embody the reality of a particular class in history (note, it does not embody the so-called "eternal human nature," i.e., the so-called "supra-historical" human, (supreme emotion)). Therefore, in this respect, it also has significance no less than form. When we speak of the content of a work, we are not only referring to the specific realistic material embodied in it, but also to the "synthesis" that the specific realistic material has expressed after its artistic value has been completed through form, that is, not only is its theme realistic, fully expressing the essence of a particular historical class, and possessing the highest degree of positivity, but its form also fully exploits the positivity of the theme, making its theme more powerfully expressed in form. Here, we not only discover the determining role of content, but also discover the positivity of form, and further confirm the inseparability of the two. The realist creative methods of classical writers are not only the expression forms of classical writers' realism, that is, the question of descriptive techniques, but also the question of how classical writers extracted their material from reality and expressed it. Therefore, this relates to the entirety of the classical writers' creative methods, rather than limiting the legacy issue to the imitation or extraction of the "style" of classical writers because "since the thoughts of classical great art are unrelated to us, then what can be our legacy should be in the form." Because what is expressed in classical works is not only the thoughts that we should not want, but also embodies the living historical truth, and the greatness of how classical writers grasped this reality and further expressed this creative method.

Therefore, we can say that Mr. Xin Ren's limitation of the legacy issue to the form of classical writers, to the point of their style, is making the issue too narrow. (End)

Passerby 219

— Yang Juan

The ship slowly comes to a stop. The muddy yellow waves on the river, beating with the leisurely rhythm of the August river wind, rush over with a "la li hua la" sound, and then ebb away.

On the deck of the small ferry picking up passengers, I begin to see the wings of the Statue of Liberty, exchanging the gentle gaze from two years ago. The setting sun, nearing dusk, passionately kisses the spire of the twenty-five-story building with the love of a witch.

The longing under the bright sky of the southern country, the yearning at the seaside, all dissipate and merge into a joyous scene when I land. The streets are filled with speeding cars, circulating like the city's blood vessels, flowing along the smooth asphalt roads like water.

Two people smoking Abdulla cigarettes with the flavor of the southern waters, dragging their melancholy figures, under the eaves painted by the setting sun, a conversation floats up with the lingering smoke:

Life is really boring, it's been almost two years.

That's right, graduated, what are you going to do?

As long as I have food, anything is fine, but I still have no idea.

After speaking, he frowned ruefully, and exhaled a puff of smoke. I don't want to say any more. Aren't we all burdened by the weight of life?

The windmill-style Dutch village, the quiet lights soaking in the surroundings, we drink strong coffee. The low walls are inlaid with Don Quixote-style medieval knight portraits and green wave patterns. The weary traveler, given this warm and gentle caress, drowsily thinks of sleep; thinks of the past, and a happy future.

From the dark sea where red and purple lights change interactively, I use whiskey to prick my nerves. The smooth surface, like gentle waves, is inlaid with the faces of various night women, some unfamiliar faces. Time slips away so quickly, the dream of youth is short, and it is pushed away in an instant. I am stunned for a moment by the melancholy of the smoke, then I walk away blowing an outdated whistle.

It is dusk again, in the blue steel of the Shanghai-Ping United Transportation at the North Station, when the flags are waved and the tears of the farewell crowd fall. I turn my head and stare at the fading figure on the platform, gradually hidden in the crowd, and say dreamily, "Good night, Shanghai!"

Autumn's Heart 220

— Yang Cunren

The era of autumn gives people an autumn heart.

If it were winter, even though the wind and snow are continuous, and the hibernating insects endure the brutal attacks, there is still the hope that spring is coming soon; but autumn, facing what is coming soon, is the winter season of wind and snow!

Autumn not only makes people melancholic, but also makes people depressed; it is a climate without love, without warmth, without hope!

This era is just like autumn: without love, without warmth, without hope. The era of Werther is past, the era of Rudin is also past, and now, it is the era of Sanin.

From struggle to disillusionment, disillusionment and then struggle again, the forward-moving heart encourages young people to straighten their spines, but in the end, they still get an emptiness, that is autumn, this era.

It is said to open our eyes and see that this era is winter, and spring is coming soon; however, in words, I can also say it, and looking at the wilderness, reality is precisely the autumn of falling leaves.

In the autumn of falling leaves, some people love her white clouds, some people love her bright moon, and some people leisurely admire the chrysanthemums under the eastern fence, but I am foreseeing the winter season of wind and snow coming soon.

Autumn's heart, a melancholic and depressed heart, a lonely and trembling heart!

Sister Pearl (Part 2) 221

— Chen Xue Zhao

After graduating from girls' elementary school, we separated. My family sent me to a girls' middle school far from my hometown. I never saw Sister Pearl again. Her shadow only appeared when I returned to my hometown during vacations, passing the post office, passing Chunhui Hall, and then sadly reflected once again in my mind. Her situation, everything about her, was completely blurred to me. I only obtained some imaginative information from inaccurate rumors. But I knew that her relationship with my cousin was still very good. My cousin and I had long since cut off contact, but after she went to school in Shanghai, she had many unsatisfactory things happen, which everyone in our hometown knew.

When I came back for the New Year and summer vacations, my mother always told me about the things that had happened during my time away from home, especially about my former female classmates.

"...Oh, speaking of Sister Pearl, she's already engaged."

"No, she's already married," my sister-in-law corrected from the side.

After that, all I knew was that she was married to a doctor who had studied at a medical school in Hangzhou, but he didn't practice medicine. He lazed around at home all day long and had a big opium addiction. The young couple rented a house from the Wang family at the back of the Zhou house. Because Sister Pearl's father-in-law was in business in Xiashi, her mother-in-law had just died, and her little sister-in-law had just gotten married. Then, Sister Pearl gave birth to a baby boy.

This time, I hadn't been back to my hometown for more than four years. By chance, at a fellow villager's wedding banquet, I met my cousin.

"How come you're also in Beiping?" She looked a little surprised to see me, and also a little ashamed, and said.

"Yes," I said, "We only have the opportunity to meet today." Suddenly, the shadow of her sworn sister flashed in my mind.

It had been fourteen years since my cousin and I left our hometown girls' elementary school, and this was the first time we had met.

"How is Sister Pearl now?" I hesitated for a moment, but finally asked.

"She's dead!" My cousin answered with a somewhat embarrassed look.

"Ah!" I couldn't help but shout. Her answer was really too far from what I had expected in my heart.

My surprise and sadness were probably involuntarily revealed. My cousin looked at me, her expression no longer as embarrassed as before, but rather calm and friendly, and said to me:

"I don't know what she died of. New Brother said it was tuberculosis."

"New Brother?"

"That's Sister Pearl's husband. He's studying medicine."

"Ah!"

After a moment, I asked:

"Isn't he an opium smoker?" I couldn't help but express my regret for Sister Pearl: "How could she want to marry an opium smoker?"

"Yes! I thought so too," then my cousin began to tell me at length about Sister Pearl's marriage to this opium fiend:

"They had been corresponding long before they got married. When people came to propose marriage, Sister Pearl's stepmother was very good and said that she didn't want to send Pearl into a den of opium, and refused. But Sister Pearl herself insisted that she had to marry him. They had already been corresponding with each other at that time. It was New Brother's sister who arranged it. I advised her not to marry this person, advised her to sell her jewelry, and also use this money to redeem books and learn some skills for independent living, and even if she wanted to marry, she could marry someone better than this. Mr. Li also came to advise her like this—Mr. Li is the female gymnastics teacher that my second brother loves, and another sworn sister of Pearl Sister—she said that she was willing to marry him, and she didn't care about the opium smoking. If she abandoned him, it would be too unjust... Actually, at that time, it was impossible for her to study. All of her jewelry had been swindled away by New Brother's sister to pay for New Brother's opium smoking."

After hearing these words, I couldn't help but feel a chill in my heart. The image of Sister Pearl who only knew how to "laugh it off" flashed in my mind, a happy Sister Pearl. However, thinking about it carefully, I felt that this kind of thing did not fall from the sky, but could be said to be made by Sister Pearl's personality. I remembered that when she and I were the best of friends, I often talked to her about going to school. I had a great desire for knowledge. But she, on the other hand, just wanted to get some things to eat, wear, and play with, and play mahjong. Other than that, she loved to read novels like "The Wobei," "The Rouge Tower," and "The Pearl Pagoda"... "If I abandon him, it would be too unjust..." How much she wanted to learn to be the heroine in this kind of novel! But what was the result? Thinking of this, I couldn't help but sigh deeply.

My cousin continued to narrate the story of Sister Pearl and them:

"When she was giving birth, I saw Sister Pearl once. She was fine at that time. Later, when I went to her house again, she was already sick. New Brother said it was tuberculosis. He also said that she wouldn't live for more than a year..."

"Then, when he saw her approaching death, didn't he think of a way to help her?"

My cousin didn't say anything, seemingly also immersed in this question.

Now, every time I go to the post office, passing Chunhui Hall, I can't help but have the shadow of Sister Pearl appear in my mind, and it also triggers a lot of consistent associations. My fourth brother, since marrying a wealthy woman, has been immersed in gambling and has completely degenerated. I thought that if my fourth brother had married Sister Pearl, he might not have degenerated, and Sister Pearl might not have died so early... However, at the end of the association, a dark curtain covered the image of Sister Pearl, who was always "laughing it off" and happy, and a sense of desolation was added to my melancholy heart.

May 16, 1934

Mr. Township Chief (28) 222

— Wang Renshu

"One case is not settled, and another case arises! I won't be the Township Chief anymore! Don't hold me back! Don't hold me back!" Mr. Feng Wen shook his head, begging for mercy. He immediately felt that the taste of "attention" and "raise the gun" was not easy to savor. And the fact that his wife looked down on him and left him to work outside was also for a reason. "New mud, met with the intercalary sixth month," wasn't it?

This time, Dong Sheng, with his crippled hand, was so scared that his face was the color of mud. After a moment of stunned silence, he fled out the back door.

Kaiyang, Ah Xian, Ah De... these people seemed unable to comprehend, standing there in a daze. As if it was they themselves, not Ah Zhao, who were killed by the bandits—no, by "numbers," by "fate."

"Amitabha! Kill the bandits a thousand times, cut the bandits ten thousand times!" Kaiyang's mother, with tears and snot, comforted Ah Zhao's wife. A face full of mud mixed with tears and snot flowed.

After finishing his last cup of wine, Old Mu Ren dragged his sandalwood tree-sized crazy foot and stepped out the door.

"Damn it! What kind of world is this!"

He cursed as he left.

Mr. Dasheng shook his head. However, he still persuaded Ah Zhao's wife, saying:

"Ah Zhao's wife! Don't make a scene anymore. People are dead, they can't come back to life. For the funeral arrangements, all expenses, the village will start donating tomorrow. In the future, I will also ask the county for a plaque, saying that Ah Zhao was a martyr, who died for the Second World War. Then you will gain both fame and fortune!"

"But, I want Ah Zhao! I want my sky! Sky... Sky!..." Then Ah Zhao's wife sat up on the ground and cried out in a long voice, with rising and falling tones!

"Damn it! What kind of world is this!"

Old Crazy Mu Ren, dragging his big crazy foot far away, also dragged this curse far away. (End)

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Confidence in National Products 223

— Yang An

Everyone knows that revolution is not as good as reforming the heart, and material construction is not as good as psychological construction. The issue of national products is also like this. It is better to have faith in national products than to promote them. If one is forced to use national products, it is better not to force it. I do not approve of some people using national products for the sake of face, and I disapprove even more of some people using national products for fear of being talked about. For all Chinese people, using Chinese goods is everyone's duty, everyone's natural gift, flowing completely from true nature, emanating completely from the bottom of one's heart, without the need for any coercion or disguise. The general unscrupulous merchants, hanging up a sheep's head to sell dog meat, filling the national products with goods from the enemy or foreign countries, are truly unforgivable and their crimes are innumerable.

Mr. Wang Jingwei recently said at the opening of the National Products Company on the Double Tenth Festival: "People who buy national products should not buy them to compare with foreign goods. Even if Chinese goods are not good, they should feel that they are better than foreign goods." These words completely arouse the confidence of our people in national products, and are truly thorough, clear, and flavorful.

Mr. Wang also said: "People who buy goods should carefully and prudently choose the goods, and not be fooled by others. Those who sell goods should choose items that are perfect, and take the idea of rights lightly." In short, for the sake of national products, both the seller and the buyer must have a kind of confidence, which develops into strength, and cannot be shaken by any ideological movement.

National Products Forum

Urgently Needed "National Goods Education" 224

— Xuan Wan

What is "National Goods Education"? My answer is that "National Goods Education" is a new type of education centered on revitalizing national goods. It uses educational methods to enlighten people's understanding of national goods and impart practical production knowledge and skills, so that people across the country can feel the importance of promoting national goods and then put their felt tasks into practice. In the educational setting, it aims to drastically change our inherent mentality of worshiping foreign goods, achieve economic self-sufficiency, balance our own production and consumption, and base the prosperity of the entire nation on this.

Therefore, what we should pay attention to here is that in the past, our efforts to promote national goods have always focused on the concrete promotion of production movements, purely relying on subjective ideals to enrich the national goods themselves and to confront rampant foreign goods. In this way, the construction of public psychology and how to use a great educational force to influence and cultivate have always been neglected. This is undoubtedly the most regrettable thing in the past.

Therefore, at present, standing at the point where the "craze for foreign goods" among our people has reached its peak, the importance of implementing national goods education has naturally become our most urgent task. Furthermore, in my opinion, its implementation path can be roughly divided into two standpoints: schools and society. The former is a place for cultivating young people across the country, while the latter is a field for the general public. The discussion is divided as follows:

1. Schools　Schools are places for cultivating the knowledge class. They are inherently responsible for inspiring children's patriotic psychology and cultivating students' noble character. So, at this time, how should we strive to expound the spirit of national goods and cultivate students? The compilation of national goods teaching materials and the promotion of national goods slogans are naturally the main aspects of national goods education.

2. Society　The scope of implementing "National Goods Education" is certainly not limited to students in schools alone. The general public in society also has the same urgency. The holding and establishment of past national goods exhibitions and national goods display halls are also a type of "National Goods Education." However, how should we use new methods in the future to increase their promotional capabilities and achieve the effect of "getting twice the result with half the effort"?

In short, in the process of national goods revitalization and production increase, the significance and mission of "National Goods Education" cannot be ignored. I sincerely hope that those engaged in the national goods movement will quickly pay attention to this point and start implementing it. Then, the day of its success will surely be the day of national economic and national industrial prosperity and revitalization!

National Goods Talk

Everyone Take Responsibility 225

— Ba Ling

This year is the National Women's National Goods Year, known throughout the country. As Chinese women, we should certainly practically use national goods. Even our male compatriots should especially practically purchase and use national goods to help women promote and produce national goods, so that China's great national goods movement can achieve great development, great success, and excellent results with the joint efforts of men and women standing on the same front.

However, while the theory is like this, what is the actual performance? Alas! It is truly enough to make us heartbroken and indignant. During the Women's National Goods Year, newspapers frequently publish news of import surpluses of various goods. I will now roughly record some of them below to prove that I am not mistaken:

(1) The imports of porcelain and chewing gum in July totaled 697,559 yuan.

(2) The import of felt hats, based on the statistics for July alone, reached 85,636 gold units, equivalent to 170,844 national currency units, a two-fold increase compared to the same period last year.

(3) The import surplus of cigarettes nationwide in August totaled 40,000,000 yuan, meaning that almost every Chinese compatriot had to bear an import surplus of one yuan.

(4) The import surplus of lace used by women to make clothes in the first half of the year was 292,195 gold units, equivalent to 577,962 national currency units.

(5) The import surplus of children's toys, according to the statistics for the past eight months, was 664,000 yuan.

(6) ...

Enough! The statistics of just a few items have already made us surprised and amazed? At the same time, they have made us very heartbroken. Alas! The result of the Women's National Goods Year is like this. This is not only a disgrace to the women's community but also a great humiliation to the entire nation, which is a very heartbreaking thing.

Now, more than two-thirds of the time for the Women's National Goods Year has passed. In the remaining seventy or eighty days, how should we strive to establish a belief in using national goods and a determination to produce national goods, and try to wash away this enormous humiliation? This responsibility should not only be shouldered by women, but we men should also practically take it up!

Popularizing the Promotion of National Goods 226

— Rong Yu

"The import of women's cosmetics in the first six months of this year was more than 800,000 yuan."

"Several ladies in this city who are enthusiastic about promoting national goods are collecting various national goods for daily use to exhibit and promote in the inland areas."

These two news items are absolutely contradictory. It is truly both joyful and fearful. There is no need to talk about fearful things, because "past events are like death"? As long as we make efforts in the future to mend the fold after the sheep is lost, there will be considerable effectiveness. So I will talk about the methods of national goods exhibitions and promotions, just for the reference of all patriotic ladies.

People in the intellectual class certainly know that promoting national goods is currently the only key to saving the country. However, ordinary low-level people do not care about national goods or not. As long as the goods are good and the price is right, they will scramble to buy them. There are many such low-level people in cities or inland areas. When we promote national goods, we should not only focus on the "bourgeoisie" but also pay attention to these low-level people. Therefore, the method of publicity must be studied carefully.

For low-level people, "text is far inferior to pictures; pictures are inferior to singing; singing is inferior to drama." This is generally accepted. When promoting national goods in inland areas or exhibiting national goods, simply relying on a few leaflets or borrowing a place to display the goods like a museum, the effect is almost zero. I think that before talking about promoting national goods, first borrow a public place to perform dramas, inviting the general public to visit. The drama should naturally depict the current poverty and weakness of the country and the harms of using foreign goods. After the public understands, then turn to the main topic, persuading the public to purchase and use national goods, and also tell them about the national goods and trademarks, so that they remember them firmly. In addition, compose some popular and simple songs and teach them to sing. If they can sing them and often say them, their minds will have another engraving. As for eye-catching pictures, they also have considerable effectiveness, so it is okay to hang them in the venue or print them into leaflets and distribute them to the public. This approach is like giving an injection of morphine to people in the intellectual class, which can also make them feel excited. For low-level people, it is a great public education to make them understand everything!

Newspaper advice and written publicity are effective in other countries. As for our noble country, there are really too few literate people; the number of people who read newspapers is also not as widespread as in other countries, so using this type of method is simply like "performing with a stone mortar on your head," a lot of effort with little return. As for performing dramas and singing songs, that is the most palatable to the general public. I think it is worth trying. It will definitely not fail; perhaps there will be unexpected gains, who knows?

National Goods Snapshot

Retrospect of the Taixian National Exhibition 227

— Yun Sun

Taixian is a small city located in the remote northern part of Jiangsu Province. This year, with the arrival of autumn, when the red leaves had not yet fallen, the party, government, business, and other organizations initiated a national goods exhibition. The scope was naturally small, only to call the attention of the men and women of the entire county! Its achievements and impressions, taken as a proportion of the entire country, are naturally just a drop in the bucket. However, just in terms of what cities are doing with "National Goods Year" and "Women's National Goods Year," and many national goods exhibitions, I am afraid that people in inland areas, even those who are active day and night in cities, cannot even translate the meaning of these words. We know the common sayings that "accumulated fur can make a robe" and "united will can build a city." The national goods movement must penetrate into the people and can absolutely not achieve long-term and far-reaching results by promoting it in a biased manner. Therefore, this small county national exhibition is worth writing about for retrospect. The address was in the Town God Temple, with two tall cypress arches erected at the east and west gates; another cypress arch was also built at Zhongshan Gate, which is busy with shops. The passersby had never seen anything so rare in their eyes, and the people who stopped to watch were shoulder to shoulder. Inside the venue, five or six courtyards of the Daxiong Hall-style houses, each with a huge courtyard, had national goods shops opening on the left and right sides of the long corridor. Every day, the tourists truly emptied the streets to come and watch, a grand event that the small city had never seen before. The giants of silk and cloth shops such as Tianchengtai, Guangtai, and Tianfu on Pozi Street occupied a large position in the venue, with temporary markets set up; rattan chair shops, medicinal material shops, cigarette shops, and porcelain bowl shops were also central displays on the spot. Cigarettes and rattan utensils were still able to attract the audience, because they had some knowledge of "showcases" and knew how to put some effort into the word "exhibition"; silk and cloth seemed too conservative; there was no new expression, giving visitors a deep impression. In Taixian, this groundbreaking great movement was a new record in the county annals. County Magistrate Zhang was still afraid that the county residents would not be enthusiastic enough to visit, so he specially hired a troupe of Hui opera and used the old theater of the Town God Temple. Everyone thought that there were free plays (without spending money) to watch, so there were always more than ten thousand people every day, actually squeezing the Town God Temple to the point where water could not leak through. I imagined that the groups hosting the exhibition would truly use the season. This new autumn is the harvest season for the general small bourgeoisie in the inland areas, and even the tenant farmers in the countryside can also have some breathing room these days to discuss marriages and add new clothes. Therefore, the national exhibition made a small fortune. I very much hope that the party and government agencies in various counties can emulate and follow up, which is a relatively practical dawn for the future of national goods.

National Goods Exhibition in Pudong District 228

— Ye Qibai

In the commercial areas of Shanghai, we know that several "National Goods Exhibitions" and temporary "National Goods Markets" have already been held. In fact, even now, there are already several fixed markets in the commercial areas of Shanghai that sell national goods, such as the one at the Tianhougong Bridge City Chamber of Commerce, the one at the original site of the Nanshi Social Affairs Bureau, and the "Penglai City Market," etc. However, in industrial areas, residential areas, and rural areas near commercial areas, large-scale "temporary national goods markets" or "national goods exhibitions" are still rare.

The creation of this "Shanghai Pudong District National Goods Exhibition" cannot but make us extremely happy. Why? Because to recover rights and interests, the most important thing is to revitalize industry; to promote national goods, the most important thing is to expand publicity. However, if we want to expand publicity in terms of time and space, then the only way is to set up "National Goods Exhibitions" everywhere. The reason why there is a "National Goods Exhibition" in Lannidu, Pudong this time is: firstly, in terms of location, although it is separated by the Huangpu River, the number of "foreign goods stores" is indeed alarming, so holding a "National Goods Exhibition" is indeed necessary; secondly, in terms of the level of school education and social education, it is not as good as Shanghai by far, so there is indeed a need to publicize the habit of purchasing and using national goods; thirdly, Lannidu is a factory area, and the population density is naturally greater than in other places; therefore, it is even more necessary to hold a "National Goods Exhibition."

This year, the author is teaching in Pudong and is even closer to this "National Goods Exhibition." I heard that in addition to exhibiting various national goods, the parties concerned have also invited students from local primary and secondary schools to hold "National Goods Speech Contests"; one is to encourage students to recognize the purchase and use of national goods; the other is to have the nature of publicity, which is a perfect method.

But I have a few hopes at the end, written below, and I hope that the parties concerned will adopt them:

1. The exhibition locations should be many, such as Gaoqiao, Wusong, Longhua, Jiangwan, etc., which all need to be held from time to time, or a fixed "National Goods Market" should be set up.

2. The exhibition time should be long, such as one month, two months, or even three months, half a year, etc.; in this way, the impression can also be deep.

3. Make the audience or buyers come in a steady stream and, moreover, increase their interest.

4. Use students and encourage students to do various effective publicity.

5. Encourage the introduction and publicity of buyers and audiences.

6. In the future, when holding this type of exhibition, there must be large-scale publicity with written and pictorial explanations.

7. As much as possible, solicit the opinions of buyers and audiences on the improvement of national goods after purchase and use, so as to improve the goods to the best of their quality.

Are the above seven points appropriate? Please correct me.

Domestically Produced Glycerin Sold Abroad 230

— Du Le

Glycerin has a wide range of uses, and many finished products have a close relationship with it. However, my country could not manufacture it on its own in the past, and the glycerin used was all foreign goods. Because the cost was high, the manufactured goods often could not compete with foreign goods!

Since the Wuzhou Second Factory created the domestically produced Planet Brand glycerin, business has been very good. Major industrial factories such as China Chemical, Yonghe, Family, Sincere, Meixing, and Huacheng in this city are all purchasing as much as possible. This is of course because it is cheap and of good quality. Recently, there has been even more gratifying news, that is, a German foreign firm has ordered 50 tons of Planet Brand glycerin from Wuzhou, preparing to send it to Mumbai, India. It is said that they will continue to order. Domestically produced scientific raw materials can be sold to foreign countries. Of course, this Planet Brand glycerin is a new example, and at the same time, its ingredients and value can be imagined.

Special Article

Research on the Subsequent Progress of Native Cloth Improvement and Promotion 231

— Jin Xiawen

Since the Taijiabao Relief Association promoted the improvement of Taicang native cloth, the process can be divided into three stages: (1) Persuading weavers to change the width of the fabric and lengthen the shuttle. (2) After the finished product is completed, explore whether there is a market, and display it for trial sales everywhere. (3) Find out the opinions of buyers, which colors are the most fashionable; whether the dimensions are appropriate. Since the autumn of the 21st year, after starting to improve from Huangjing Township in Taicang, after many days and research by comrades, the three problems have been gradually resolved until this spring. (1) The villagers originally regarded weaving cloth as a sideline, but because the sales of native cloth were cut off, they had to wait for death. Now that they can lend yarn to weave cloth and earn wages to make a living, no matter how wide the fabric is or how long the shuttle is, once the improvement is advertised, there is no need to persuade them. They come one after another, taking yarn to weave cloth. This first problem is the easiest to solve. (2) Since we started to improve native cloth, all comrades have been worried about the difficulty of sales. If there is no way to sell it, then the finished goods will pile up like a mountain, and if one piece is worth one yuan, ten thousand gold can be used up immediately. However, we have great courage, thinking that cloth is incomparable to other things. Even if there is no way to sell it, we can use it ourselves if there are goods in stock. So we tried our best to promote it, and Mr. Pan Yangyao introduced it for sale at the National Goods Market. The first time, the appetite was still good, but after two or three times, the stomach was dull and sales were slow, and the price of goods fell sharply. Later, we discussed with the Native Cloth Store of the Shanghai County Farmers Education Center to sell it on consignment, but it was not very prosperous either. However, this rural native cloth has been able to be displayed in the Shanghai market and worn by patriotic men and women in Shanghai. We are very fortunate in our hearts, thinking that sales are guaranteed, but sooner or later. This spring, a relative returned from Haizhou, who is patriotic and took the responsibility of selling native cloth to the Longhai area. He took all the goods accumulated in Taicang and Shanghai and went away. In less than three months, all the goods were remitted back, urging to send the goods and saying, "The more the better." But because the stock has been exhausted, the weaving households have temporarily stopped due to the busy farming season, and there is no way to cope with it. From then on, the second problem can be solved. (3) For Shanghai tailors, ant seat flower has been tired of the old, and need to change patterns more; colors need to use the shade Stanlin does not fade and is bright, the most appropriate, the size of the cloth, with a foot four inches wide, used to make women's cheongsam, can be uniquely tailored without hemming, the shuttle is two feet three inches, || can make two cheongsams. The selling price of each piece is one yuan and four corners, then each piece is only seven corners, and the economy is more cost-effective. As for Haizhou, sales are not the same. The soil cloth of Changshu Taicang (Huangjing) is only eight inches wide. Now the width is one foot three inches, the sleeves are not found, and the trouser legs are not very angled, which is already suitable. As for the color, it can still be casual now, but after a year or two, I am afraid it will have to be improved ||| The third problem can also come to an end. Therefore, three problems have been solved; and then further research is done. In our Taicang twenty-five townships, more than half of them can weave cloth. Now we start from Huangjing Township; and choose 40 weaving households in one township to try out, lending yarn to weave cloth. Each household weaves one piece a day, and one month produces 1,200 pieces. The total cost needs 1,640 yuan. If it is sold to Haizhou, the cost will be more than 4,800 yuan to settle the account at the festival. The machine continues to spin and weave, and another batch of goods must be prepared, then the capital will be nearly 10,000. If it is expanded to the whole county, then it will be added again and again. At present, the finished goods can not lose money. If you eat the village money, add the interest on the demolition, then the native cloth will have to increase in price, and the sales will be affected, then the cost will become a big problem. ||| The Haizhou area. Four hundred miles around, this is a prosperous area for the sale of foreign cloth. Now, under the influence of promoting national goods and publicity, patriotic enthusiasm is surging. Occasionally, when you see the improved native cloth on the market, you are enthusiastically buying it. Therefore, the shipments from Taicang Huangjing; together with the products from Shanghai Zhuanqiao, are continuously sent, which is not enough for the sales of Haizhou alone: In fact, patriotic men and women in Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Hangzhou, Beiping, Tianjin, Shandong and other places who use native cloth are definitely not a few. As long as there is a solution to the economic problem, it is not difficult to sell it widely; as for the width, color, and improvement methods, it is impossible to do it all at once, but it is also impossible not to study. The fabric of the hand-woven fabric is only one foot four or five inches wide. If it is changed to a pulling shuttle, the width can be two feet. The width of two feet is the most suitable for the Shanghai market. Now, in order to maintain the family handicraft industry and relieve the rural areas, we have to improve the existing throwing shuttle weaving households, and in the future, we will definitely want to send each weaving household a pulling shuttle cloth machine to let them learn. As for dyeing without fading, it is necessary to use German Shade Stanlin, but how can the material be used without waste; how to set the color brightly, learning the operation is not easy, this is also for further research in the future, shallow like me, has been stored in my heart for a long time, I have to take the process and research, to the national goods experts, Shangqi not stingy to guide Fortunately!

Foreign Exchange: Brisk Buying, Marked by Rising Gold Prices

Someone Sells Bars, Still Rises Twelve Yuan

Already More Than Twenty Yuan Above the Standard Price

Yesterday's gold market saw sustained robust buying and unusually depleted supplies on the trading floor. Despite occasional supply of bars from certain parties, the situation was like a small amount of porridge for many monks, making it difficult to stem the overall trend. Chinese merchants continued to buy aggressively, putting pressure on banks. As a result, the exchange market, both officially and unofficially, tightened repeatedly, and the upward trend became even more pronounced. Overseas silver markets and the standard gold prices quoted by international telecommunications central banks had little impact on the sentiment of fellow traders. The market trend for half the day remained dominated by buyers, repeatedly breaking through the 56, 60, and 70 yuan marks. Early in the morning, foreign dispatches indicated stable British and rising American silver markets, also boosting exchange rates. However, due to a slight retraction of three and a half pence in the London pure gold price, sentiment softened slightly. Pre-market trading opened lower at 44-45 yuan, but buyers still actively stepped in, immediately pushing the price above 50 yuan. After the opening, the Central Bank's announced rates showed stable British and rising American silver by 1.25, Customs Gold falling by 0.04, and the standard gold price decreasing to 941.9 yuan. This caused temporary market hesitation and a dip, but sellers lacked strength, and the price stabilized after the drop. Ultimately, because the Central Bank's quoted price differed greatly from the market price, it was difficult to maintain confidence. The market soon turned bullish again, and the gold market also rebounded. The exchange market remained strong. HSBC's quoted rates narrowed again, triggering selling pressure, but a lack of suppliers caused it to break above 60 yuan. Although there was a pullback, the overall trend remained one of demand exceeding supply, with extremely scarce funding. The flour market rose immediately at the opening in the morning, and continued to rise in the afternoon. It expanded in each round, and the increase was very rapid. It also attracted the attention of silver and money industries and new bulls inside and outside the industry, resulting in a soaring market. Recent factory short covering was especially strong. However, in reality, large-scale actual sales are still waiting and seeing. The rise in market prices is entirely due to people's good expectations and floating stockholders competing to buy. Closing price: 9.75 cents higher for this month, 7.5 cents higher for next month, 5.75 cents higher for December, 6 cents higher for January, and 6.25 cents higher for February.

The wheat market rose because foreign wheat futures rose by 5 and 12 cents. The gold price rose, and spot wheat also saw a rise. Fixed wheat did not decline. People's hearts were upward. After the opening, there were outside bulls and floating stockholders buying. Short covering was especially strong. Therefore, after the opening price, each month immediately rose by 34 cents to 67 cents. Subsequently, it was reduced by bulls closing out positions. However, there were still customers for the long term. At the close, this month and next month were 2 cents higher each, December was 1 cent higher, January was 4 cents higher, and February was 6 cents higher. Spot wheat was bid up step by step. Yesterday, more than 1,000 bags of trucked wheat arrived, and the price was 10 cents higher, opening at 3.50 yuan, 3.50 yuan, and then 3.45 yuan.

Chicago wheat and corn were both strong. The report of the Bureau of Agricultural Economics stated that based on the domestic situation, market prices would be high. As a result, all parties engaged in purchasing. Generally, they ignored the threats of government intervention in coarse grain trading. Bad harvest news and tight livestock feed conditions made the coarse grain market strong. Rumor has it that due to the shortage of feed, wheat will be used to feed cattle and sheep. The grain industry believes that the high market price is no longer a problem.
