Little West Heaven 245

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Third Episode: Not Understanding Drifting, Peeking at the Door to Pity the Young Girl; Willing to Hear Suffering, Cherishing Jade, Visiting a Poor Family

That girl raised her eyelids, looked at him, smiled, and flashed her body under the eaves pillar. That small-footed woman followed behind and said: Don't you want to take another look? Why are you running? The girl smiled and said: There are so many people, running into someone else's house is quite embarrassing, let's go, I won't look anymore. The small-footed woman ignored her and gave the waiter a look. The waiter stood at the door and looked at Zhang Jiefu in the room again. Seeing the smile on his face, he said to the small-footed woman: Since he doesn't want to look anymore, take him to the front building to play. After a while, I will send the clothes to your home. The woman smiled and nodded, and took the girl away. As soon as they left, discussions began here. Li Shilian smiled and said: She is really a top-notch person. If she is groomed a little, she is sure to be a talent of upper-middle class. Zhang Jiefu had a cigarette in his mouth, walked out in slippers, and smiled at Cheng Zhiqian and said: I am acting on the spot. I heard that this girl had no luck finding relatives and wanted to sell herself to rely on two generations of people. I thought this girl had a heart and mind, so I wanted to take a look. What Brother Li said is right, we are here to seek a career, how can we do absurd things. Cheng Zhiqian sighed and felt that it was wrong, and smiled again. Zhang Jiefu didn't know what he meant, so he said to the waiter: We can't let people come for nothing. See how much money to give him? Saying that, he reached into his clothes pocket to touch it. The waiter smiled and said: Money is not necessary. This Hu family's sister-in-law said that this child has a family of three, and she is a young widow, how can she afford it. I just hope to quickly find someone for this girl, as the third wife or the second wife, it doesn't matter. He has a grandma and a mother, and it's enough to have food to eat. Cheng Zhiqian shook his head with both hands in his suit pants and said: This may be difficult. If you are the second or third wife, there must be a big wife on top. Whether the person can accommodate it is still a problem. Who can guarantee to support two generations of his family? (42)

Defending Zhang Fei 246

— Sha Yongcai

When it comes to Zhang Huanhou of the Three Kingdoms, there is really no one who doesn't know him. According to the folklore, his dignified appearance is the ancestor of ugly men with black faces and curly beards. According to the legend, his temperament is a reckless Heavenly Venerable who is furious. These two characteristics of him are also like his famous name, lasting for thousands of years. Anyone who looks at the stage and sits in the book hall has such an image in his mind about him.

However, according to the textual research in the official history, Huanhou's appearance and temperament are not as bad as the folk legend. According to the biography of Zhang Fei in the Biography of Famous Officials in the ancient version: His behavior is described as "swallowing jaw and ring eyes, and his appearance is very great." It can be seen that he is only a little different from ordinary people in the jaw and eyes. His temperament is "fierce and refreshing, with quick wit, and often has many surprising strategies in every battle." It can be seen that he is not only not irritable, but also has talent and wisdom, and is not a reckless man who does not know a single character. Probably the reason why later generations mistakenly passed him as a reckless Heavenly Venerable is because of misunderstanding the two words "fierce and refreshing."

In the area of ​​Langzhong County in northern Sichuan Province, Huanhou was originally the garrison during the Shu Han Dynasty, and his tomb is still there. Therefore, there are many Huanhou temples there, and the statues in the temples are mostly dignified and solemn, not full of soot-like scary faces. This is in line with the records in the historical records. Recently, according to a report in the Beiping newspaper, Mr. Jin, the president of the Lake Society, said that "Zhang Fei of the Shu Han Dynasty was good at painting, and he was especially good at painting beauties, and he was also good at calligraphy. His calligraphy was elegant and vigorous. Now it can still be found in ancient steles." According to this, Huanhou is not only rich in talent and wisdom, but also has more elegant things. It is only because the historical records rarely record this item, and the folk romances have too much exaggeration, which makes thousands of years later, fabricated and attached, all losing the truth, which is regrettable!

Most of the small toys are actually foreign goods, and more than 570,000 yuan of gold has flowed into the pockets of foreigners in a period of half a year! Is this the fault of the children? Taking Pictures 248

— Chen Liang

I have never been very happy to take pictures in my life. I often point out that the technicians who take pictures are invaders of freedom. If their aesthetic concepts are indeed brilliant, then I will also be convinced. Standing, they must make people stand straight, like a stalagmite. Sitting, they must make people put their right leg on their left leg, and forcibly call them elegant even if they are not elegant. If they don't smile, they must pretend to smile, and if they smile, they are not allowed to show their teeth. How to put their heads and how to stretch their feet, they must listen to their command. The photo studio's photo studio is less free and more oppressed than the command headquarters' detention center. It is not wise to spend money to buy hardship.

Many of my friends are "modern youths". In addition to 14K gold fountain pens, Zeiss platinum glasses, flat watches, etc., they are each equipped with a camera. Everyone thinks that I will often have the opportunity to take pictures without spending money. However, this is a big mistake. Because my friends all take art as their standpoint, and ugliness like mine does not meet the conditions of art at all. People who study photography art, in addition to scenery, still life, and livestock, should use women as the most suitable materials. Therefore, women enjoy the exclusive right to free photography. Whenever I travel and play in the wild, I see my friends taking all kinds of poses with their girlfriends, and I can't help but feel "I hate not being born as a daughter."

People who take the most pictures in the world should be dignitaries and movie stars. Yesterday, I visited the City God Temple and saw that all the photo studios took photos of dignitaries and stars and hung them on the door, and wrote "Special Price Reduction" and other words next to them as an advertisement to attract customers. Those who saw it found it interesting.

Boredom and Envy 249

— Moon

Wild Tea 250

— Zhu Shaofei

Probably anyone who has been to our East Mountain in spring and autumn has to go up the mountain to taste the unique wild tea. In spring, there are birds singing and flowers are fragrant, and in autumn, there are red maple leaves, full of picturesque poetry, making people reluctant to leave.

The specialty of East Mountain, such as Before the Rain and Biluochun, are fine buds like silver threads. When you brew a cup, it tastes delicious. It is very elegant to drink wild tea with these two kinds of tea leaves. The stove is built of stones, the firewood can be picked up on the spot, and the water is taken from the clear stream in the mountain stream.

The address is often in front of the tombs of ordinary people, or in deeper mountain valleys. Xinmiao's Shou tomb is recommended in the front mountain, and Xuejiawu in Chawanwu is recommended in the back mountain. These two places are good places to drink wild tea, because there are smooth stone tables and stone benches, and lush pine and cypress trees. If you are in high spirits, bring a card and play a few rounds of mahjong. You can both taste the spring and taste the tea, and you can also travel and play. It kills two birds with one stone. Why not do it?

These days, I happened to be returning to my hometown, and I met two or three childhood friends, and agreed to go to Xuejiawu to drink wild tea every afternoon after lunch. No one had the interest to play cards. Each of us took our favorite books, newspapers, magazines, and all the necessary copper pots and tea cups, and stepped on the rugged mountain road with brisk steps. Arrived at the destination!

Taking turns to start the fire, fetch water, and pick up firewood, in a blink of an eye, the water in the pot was boiling. Each child brews a cup. So. Those who read books read books, and those who take a walk take a walk, until the sun sets and the birds and animals return to their nests, then they return with great interest.

Records of Fragrant Clouds 251

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Our family is also his direct descendant, but because there are too many branches passed down, we are not very valued. Just look at this ready-made explanation. The Empress Dowager is a descendant of the Yehe Nara clan. In the past, the Yehe Nara clan can be said to have absolutely no important position. Until the demise of the Qing Dynasty, there was no second person in their clan worth paying attention to except for Empress Dowager Cixi alone. 丨丨 and as for me, although on the surface, no one can deny that I am a direct descendant of Nurhaci, but now I am serving the Empress Dowager in the palace, and some people are secretly praising me. It can be said that the situation is changing a lot, and it is difficult to predict personnel matters!

Small Recipe

Japanese Cuisine (Below) 253

— Bingyu

After drinking, you can take the dishes with chopsticks (Japanese chopsticks are disinfected, sealed in paper bags, unpacked when used, and the chopsticks are taken out. The chopsticks are made of wood, one end is cut into two branches, and the other end is connected. Use both hands to pull them apart.) The second time the main dishes are served, each person will be sent a rice bucket. You must not chew loudly when eating, showing a hungry ghost appearance. When taking a bowl to drink soup, you should specify a pair of hands and do not change them from left to right. After the fourth dish is served, the guests should thank the host for their kindness, and then choose to eat from the dishes on the plate as you like. Because there are many dishes, they cannot all be eaten. If you cannot eat them, you can leave the third and fourth dishes uneaten, and only eat some fragrant things (such as lettuce, radish pickles, etc.). After eating, hot water will be brought, and the female servant will use hot water to rinse the rice bowl. The rice crumbs in the rice bowl and the hot water are eaten together.

(2) A slightly formal banquet dish This is an ordinary banquet held in a restaurant. The order of serving dishes is first soup, then two dishes, then three dishes, and finally the main dish. Wine is served before the dishes, so you can pour and drink as you like. However, the menu varies according to the situation of each store. Usually, appetizers are served first (there are salty, sour, sweet, and spicy varieties, packed in a divided pot, allowing guests to take whatever they like). At this time, guests should take some of each dish, indicating that they like to eat everything. The second course is soup and sashimi (sashimi is a kind of raw fish slices, called Sesimi by the Japanese). When eating sashimi, do not use chopsticks to grab the back of the fish body and dip it in soy sauce before eating. The third course is grilled fish. Grilled fish can be whole or sliced. If it is whole meat, you can use chopsticks to remove the fish bones in the middle before eating. Secondly, there are boiled dishes, added dishes, etc., which are served one after another. When eating boiled dishes, you must not stick the eggs and tofu to the edge of the bowl. The next course is rice. The rice at the banquet is slightly different from the rice when eating the main dishes. The rice at the banquet is sent out last, with miso soup (cooked with fish flour, miso, and green onions) and fragrant things served together. After eating the rice, tea and a towel are sent up. At this time, the guests should politely say, "The dishes are very good, I am very full, thank you very much.

(3) How to eat a single dish Usually, when you go to the home of a middle-class friend, you will be treated with simple dishes. Other ordinary restaurants also have them. However, the single dishes made in restaurants are mostly casual and not very tasty. The oriental restaurants (Oryori) along Wusong Road and North Sichuan Road in this city are all treasures of this kind of dish, for example (1) "Sukiyaki" uses beef, chicken, green vegetables, tofu, winter bamboo shoots, green onions, soy sauce, sugar, etc. mixed together (there are also seasonal variations, probably with beef and chicken as the main ingredients) and is temporarily cooked and eaten on the table, and everyone eats it together in one pot at will. When eating, first take out the cooked vegetables from the pot with chopsticks and dip them in raw eggs (2) Dongpuriri, called well, is a large bowl of rice dishes, with various kinds of dishes and rice mixed together, such as raw fish, chicken, clams, yams, shrimp, sesame, seaweed, and other kinds, also depending on the season) similar in style to our country's Babao rice. (3) Sisi is a large plate filled with fish, meat, vegetables, mixed rice, sauce, vinegar, etc. When eating, it should be divided into small plates from the large plate. If you think the taste is light, you can dip it in the soy sauce dish first before eating.

(4) The combination of bento Bento is a simple meal prepared by Japanese people when they go out to work or go to school, and is placed in a nickel-plated box or a box made of wood chips. There are many styles of matching rice and dishes, some with mixed rice and dishes, and some with separate rice and dishes. You can match them as you like according to your favorite foods. There are ready-made ones sold at various train stations in Japan. The prices are also high and low depending on the materials used.

(5) New Year's rice in January When you go to a Japanese home to celebrate the New Year, they will first take out Fucha (tea) and snacks (fruit soup cake). When drinking tea, you should eat the tea in the teacup in two or three mouthfuls. Secondly, Tosu wine is served. There are three sets of wine cups for pouring Tosu, from small to large (Japanese wine cups are numbered one, two, and three. The one on the top is number one, which is a small cup, the one in the middle is a medium cup, and the one on the bottom is a large cup). People with large amounts of alcohol can drink as they please. After drinking Tosu wine, there is soup (cooked with seaweed and bird meat). This soup can be divided into small bowls to eat. According to the rules, it should be eaten all up and no leftovers should be left.

Shanghai Newspaper Local Supplement

On Elegance 254

— Chen Tianshe

One day at a certain hour, I forgot to bring newspapers and magazines to the toilet. Daydreaming, I went from chrysanthemums to Tao Yuanming, from Tao Yuanming to nobility, and then to elegance. So, let's talk about elegance.

Elegance is easy to talk about, but difficult to practice. Things like not cutting your hair for a year, not bathing for six months, reading alone in the deep mountains, inscribing words on high peaks, being able to eat five bowls of rice but still feigning three parts sick, etc., are beyond the reach of ordinary vulgar people. Roughly speaking, elegant people must have unique personalities.

China is originally a country of ancient elegance. In the four seasons and eight festivals, there are always elegant things to be found. "Spring outings on fragrant grasslands, summer appreciation of green lotus ponds, autumn meals with chrysanthemum wine, winter recitations of white snow poems." The moon in the middle of the ninth month does not appear as bright as in the middle of the eighth month, so appreciation is useless. But as the Mid-Autumn Festival passes and the Double Ninth Festival arrives, the act of "climbing high" may not be less elegant than "moon appreciation"! We cannot regard "Meng Jia losing his hat" as a story of fleeing in panic, because now there are "concessions," and "climbing mountains and ascending heights" should be included in elegant activities. Even the most unbearable vulgar fellows will be transformed if they just blow in the mountain breeze.

A person who has become perfectly pure in elegance will pace back and forth in the Rising Sun Building. When he receives a death announcement, he will write lyrical poems on it. Even if four more provinces are lost, he will remain indifferent, because in the circle of elegance, there are no such things as saving the country, joining the army, or sacrificing oneself. Therefore, "national affairs" are best left to "who cares." The places that elegant gentlemen frequent are nothing more than famous mountains and great rivers, teahouses and taverns, gardens and opera stages. The things that elegant gentlemen often do are nothing more than enjoying the moon and reciting poetry, treading on snow to seek plum blossoms, drinking wine and tasting tea, etc. I will not list them in detail.

In this so-called "poetic autumn," chrysanthemums are blooming and crabs are plump. They will inevitably be burdened to "steal leisure from busy times" to engage in the elegant activity of "holding crabs and admiring chrysanthemums." When talking about chrysanthemums, one must mention "Eastern Fence," and "round navels in September, pointed in October" must be recited fluently. The vision of "noble" people is of course also detached from the vulgar. They only consider that a pair of crab claws that can pinch people meet the requirements of "elegance." If you hold the crab's body to look at chrysanthemums, or hold the crab's claws to admire roses, you will cause a great illogical joke and few will not scold you as a vulgar person!

It is said that a truly elegant person has not a single vulgar bone in their body. This of course requires physiologists to study, but that kind of calm and unrestrained demeanor is indeed rare and valuable.

Under the Setting Sun 255

— Chen Liang

"Evening Post Evening Post"

A sound like scraping a clay pot.

"Half-past five" on the clock in the office, on the driver's train watch, on the comprador's "Cyma."

In the soft yellow light of the setting sun, in the tide of people rushing out of the office, there is a small, thin head, shouting with a dry, raspy voice. Hopeful eyes are filled with moisture, fixing their gaze on those in Western suits, those sitting in private cars. But few are caught. Many people glance at the headlines on the cover and run away.

Some beautiful young people just stand in front of the large glass window looking at the cheap goods.

The setting sun climbs onto every piece of metal, shooting out countless needles that prick the shallow eyelids of people. Diamond rings, miniature cameras, J4K large-sized vacuum fountain pens, autumn wool sweaters... Watching, watching, many people weave a dream of material vanity on their shallow eyelids.

The current drought and the extreme danger of the 1936 world war are things they are separated from.

However, the child, as dirty as a mangy dog, runs down the street shouting as loud as he can, carrying the evening paper. He and the hearts of all passersby are separated.

The yellow setting sun is plastered on the white tile wall of the coffee shop. Thick and thin leg shadows move on it, so chaotic and hurried. People coming out of the office come here to rest for a while. "Borsalino" hats and flannel jackets are hung on the coat rack by the white-clothed waiter. They order an evening tea, coconut cake and Brazilian coffee, and let the red lips of the female staff swallow the fatigue of the day, revealing exotic teenage sensuality. The coffee is so strong.

But the mangy-dog-like child selling the evening paper shouts even louder, with a tremor, with a taste of sorrow, "Evening Post"

"Ghost, evil ghost, endlessly noisy, get out!" From the second-floor window across the street comes an angry face with gold-rimmed glasses. The child selling the evening paper immediately knows he is being chased away. He is often threatened by the foreign bosses in that real estate company. He instinctively lowers his head, looking at the setting sun covering his feet. He discovers that his feet are starting to move towards a side street with no sunlight.

The people in the office have all left. Only the large wall calendar with landscape paintings, the typewriter, the hourglass bottle rack, the steel stationery box... accompany the loneliness of the evening.

On the street, quietly, a new streamlined car crawls past like a beetle, without a sound. From the coffee shop come graceful steps, fluttering silver silk skirt corners, fluttering brown ties. Foreign soldiers, two or three, five or six, come in waves, waving leather whips, humming "li la li la" endlessly. The setting sun is trampled blurred and faded under their leather whips.

The child selling the evening paper bursts back onto the street, shouting, "Evening Post..." Standing on the street corner like a fossil, a person who has lost inspiration, his life is blurred, faded.

On a Child Who Lost His Father in Autumn 256

— Buyang

Autumn falls entirely on the child who has lost his father.

Gray encounters, gray clothes, a gray soul, everything is immersed in a gray dye vat.

Tears constantly moisten his gloomy face, like the sky during autumn rain.

He is a melancholic person in a season full of melancholy!

Three months ago, he was still a very energetic young man. He lived happily, lightly spending carefree years. He was interested in everything. In the entire history of his life (twenty-one years), there was no autumn, although he also wore autumn clothes sometimes.

He hated autumn like he hated a sentimental and sickly woman. Unpredictable weather can be tested with a woman!

But on the day he rushed five hundred miles in one breath, on the day his father stepped into another world, he lost all the happiness he had previously enjoyed; even his only pride perished with it.

From that day on, he began to gradually come into contact with the season he had previously hated.

It was not voluntary; it was a kind of orphan's sorrow being forcibly executed.

So, a layer of gloomy gauze like that of a pregnant woman covered his spring-like face. Tears, which were originally not easily found, are now like dew in the autumn night, everywhere to be seen.

Leaning on the half table by the window, supporting his chin with both hands, he turned his watery eyes to look at the sky: the sky was heavy and gray, and fine rain like tears was falling. Perhaps it was sympathizing with him! Thinking this, he felt a trace of comfort in his heart.

Autumn is suitable for sharing hardships, he admits.

So, the autumn that he had once expressed hatred for and that was forcibly executed, he now felt a sense of favor for. He felt that he should make a living in the bleak fallen leaves and the desolate cicada sounds. He felt that he should find a way out in the autumn wind and rain.

This was a view he had personally experienced. He was glad that he could find a lover to confide in, in the lonely depths of the night.

That's how he involuntarily got engaged to a sentimental and sickly woman.

That's how, unconsciously, the elements of autumn passed through his whole body.

Page 22

On the Pasture 257

— Youhan

Everything is moving on the pasture. The cow's tail wags with extra vigor, and mosquitoes swarm in the air: it's dusk.

Xiao He, like a dog, rolls around on the pasture; his body is so light that he rolls across half the pasture in one go. Only then does his head feel a little dizzy. He turns over, stands up, looks around with his eyes, raises his voice, and shouts sharply:

"Fuck your mother, Xiao Mu!"

The cow named Xiao Mu hears this and hastily drops the mustard flower from its mouth, and runs out of the vegetable garden as if fleeing for its life, dragging its tail.

Xiao He rushes over, seizes Xiao Mu's nose ring, and sends a whip hard into the cow's belly. The cow endures the pain, turns its body several times, moves its feet lightly, and utters a pleading "Ooh!"

Xiao He gets his breath back, releases the cow's nose ring; straightens his arms, which are exactly level with the cow's back, presses down, and mounts the cow's back.

The cow continues to lower its head to graze; Xiao He hangs his limbs down, lies on his back on the cow's back, hums a Red Lotus Song, and stares at the clean evening sky, thinking in his heart: "A Ying begged..."

Twilight and evening breeze added a little together.

"Xiao He! Xiao He!" A Ying finally came; Xiao He's heart jumped, and he slid down the grass from the cow's back.

Over there, under the sycamore tree, A Ying stood there waving: "Come here, Xiao He."

"You come here," Xiao He squatted on the grass laughing; but didn't go over.

"Don't be like that! Come quickly, I have something to tell you," it was an urgent voice, her face a little red, not smiling.

Seeing that A Ying was really not joking, Xiao He's heart jumped heavily again; no longer hesitating, he ran towards her against the wind.

When the two pairs of hands clasped, the four dimples did not appear at the same time as in the past; Xiao He didn't wait to sit down and asked nervously:

"What's the matter, tell me quickly!"

Pouting her mouth, frowning her brows, she replied together: "Dad is going to sell me"

"Sold?!" Xiao He half believed and half didn't believe it.

"Yes!"

"Really? How do you know?"

"Mom told me," her mouth pouted even more severely, "She said Dad owes money to Master Xue in the city, and he can't pay it back; yesterday Master Xue sent someone to our house to collect the debt again, and Dad had no choice but to agree to send me to him as a maid, as a way to pay off the debt."

That's right, Xiao He understood now. Yesterday, when he was driving the cow past A Ying's door, he saw a city person pounding on the table in her house, scolding like thunder, and A Ying's Dad stood aside trembling.

"Oh!" He was stunned, he couldn't see anything in front of him, "When are you going?" he asked; but in his heart, he always thought that A Ying could at least play with him for a few more days.

"Tomorrow morning, Dad will take me away."

"Just tomorrow?" he asked so loudly, it sounded like a shout. "Tomorrow!" How sour this was! So sour that the two tender hearts could no longer bear it, so, round and round tears rolled down their red little cheeks, rolled down, rolled down.

For a long time, they were silent; the wind rolled their hair.

Suddenly, a hope flashed through Xiao He's mind, and his heart suddenly warmed up. He suddenly asked:

"Can you escape back?"

Being asked this suddenly, she hesitated for a moment. Many difficulties that children could think of appeared before her eyes. Finally, she shook her head and replied:

"No, I don't know the way!"

"Then!" Xiao He thought of the road; the road! How far it was! He stopped talking.

"What?" she asked, chasing closely, asking eagerly.

However, he couldn't answer. Disappointment. The two faced each other; there were no words, only tears rolling. Finally, they bumped heads and cried loudly.

The pasture was so vast, the sound of crying dissipated in the air.

Dusk reached its end. The sky, except for a white corner in the west; the rest was gray and dark. In the center of the pasture, the cow, full of grass, raised its head, looked around at the vast atmosphere, and uttered a long "Ooh..." in search of its owner's return.

Mr. Shen Shimai's Sketches 258

Curses, Part Two 259

— Xiaolin

The metropolis at night is like a promiscuous prostitute, half-naked, shamelessly throwing seductive smiles, teasing smiles at people. Many people, like this, become neurotic, go crazy, and bury their entire souls and minds in that desolate bewitching array.

Using gold to buy false pleasure, to buy the intoxication of time, in the high-speed oscillation of intoxication, without thought, one becomes a sensory machine, inseparable from the sensual enjoyment of material desires. Everything else does not exist in the eyes, not even oneself.

The night of the metropolis is an endless exchange of human desire mixed with the power of money. In the ballroom, under the dim red lights, the world suddenly shrinks to the size of you and me. Gold blooms, and carnal desire overflows. Life is seen as light as a goose feather, as ethereal as a cloud! As if if you miss today, there will be no tomorrow. So sin is regarded as proper, sending oneself to hell, wasting life to the fullest, and dissipating the days in promiscuity. These people who come and go to the colorful places are mostly burdens or outliers between people. Zombies with only a body and no soul. Living off inheritances, the content of their lives is ugly, decadent, which is equal to chronic suicide for themselves, and invisibly creates many evils for others.

Not knowing day, not knowing night, muddling through life, daily life cannot be separated from luxurious material supplies, so they are slaves of matter, prisoners of matter, and have no spiritual nourishment at all. However, they are considered to be upper-class figures in society, stepping on people's heads, basely stealing life. Their existence, although undeniable, is worthless, far less dignified than the life of a so-called lower-class person who works hard with his own hands to earn his own living.
